#Curtiss 1: Airline status

curtiss.1 = {
	type = country_event
		
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		curtiss_has_airline = yes
	}

	immediate = {

		if = {
			limit = {
				var:curtiss_flight_route <= 2
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_1_modifier
				}
			}
			add_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_1_modifier
			remove_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_2_modifier
			remove_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_3_modifier
			remove_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_4_modifier
			remove_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_5_modifier
			remove_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_6_modifier
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:curtiss_flight_route >= 3
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_2_modifier
					var:curtiss_flight_route >= 6
				}
			}
			add_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_2_modifier
			remove_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_1_modifier
			remove_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_3_modifier
			remove_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_4_modifier
			remove_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_5_modifier
			remove_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_6_modifier
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:curtiss_flight_route >= 6
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_3_modifier
					var:curtiss_flight_route >= 9
				}
			}
			add_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_3_modifier
			remove_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_1_modifier
			remove_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_2_modifier
			remove_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_4_modifier
			remove_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_5_modifier
			remove_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_6_modifier
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:curtiss_flight_route >= 9
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_4_modifier
					var:curtiss_flight_route >= 12
				}
			}
			add_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_4_modifier
			remove_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_1_modifier
			remove_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_2_modifier
			remove_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_3_modifier
			remove_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_5_modifier
			remove_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_6_modifier
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:curtiss_flight_route >= 12
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_5_modifier
					var:curtiss_flight_route >= 15
				}
			}
			add_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_5_modifier
			remove_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_1_modifier
			remove_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_2_modifier
			remove_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_3_modifier
			remove_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_4_modifier
			remove_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_6_modifier
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:curtiss_flight_route >= 15
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_6_modifier
				}
			}
			add_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_6_modifier
			remove_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_1_modifier
			remove_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_2_modifier
			remove_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_3_modifier
			remove_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_4_modifier
			remove_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_5_modifier
		}
	}
}

#Curtiss 10: Seaplanes [Schneider's Trophy JE]

curtiss.10 = {
	type = country_event

    title = curtiss.10.t
		
    desc = curtiss.10.d

	flavor = curtiss.10.f

	duration = 1
		
	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/curtiss_pictures/curtiss_schneider_foundation.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airplane"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_aviation.dds"

	trigger = {
		has_technology_researched = curtiss_seaplanes_tech
		country_rank >= rank_value:major_power
		any_scope_building = {
			is_building_type = building_port
			count >= 3
		}
		NOT = {
			has_global_variable = curtiss_seaplanes_invented
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = curtiss_seaplanes_invented
		set_global_variable = {
			name = curtiss_seaplane_nations
			value = 0
		}
	}

	option = { #A noble idea.
		name = curtiss.10.g
		add_journal_entry = {
			type = je_curtiss_found_schneider_trophy
		}
	}
}

#Curtiss 11: Has Seaplanes tech [hidden]

curtiss.11 = {
	type = country_event
		
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		has_technology_researched = curtiss_seaplanes_tech
		has_global_variable = curtiss_seaplanes_invented
		NOT = {
			has_variable = curtiss_seaplanes_country_var
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = curtiss_seaplanes_country_var
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_building = {
					is_building_type = building_port
					count >= 3
				}
				country_rank >= rank_value:major_power
			}
			change_global_variable = {
				name = curtiss_seaplane_nations
				add = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

#Curtiss 12: Henri Fabre

curtiss.12 = {
	type = country_event

    title = curtiss.12.t
		
    desc = curtiss.12.d

	flavor = curtiss.12.f

	duration = 1
		
	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/curtiss_pictures/curtiss_fabre.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airplane"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_aviation.dds"

	trigger = {
		game_date >= 1909.1.1
		NOT = {
			game_date >= 1914.1.1
		}
		NOT = {
			has_global_variable = curtiss_henri_fabre_happened
		}
		OR = {
			country_has_primary_culture = cu:french
			country_has_primary_culture = cu:occitan
			country_has_primary_culture = cu:north_italian
		}
		any_scope_state = {
			state_region = s:STATE_PROVENCE #Marseille
		}
		has_technology_researched = curtiss_early_aviation_tech
	}

	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = curtiss_henri_fabre_happened
	}

	option = { #I love this flying boat!
		name = curtiss.12.g
		default_option = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_technology_researched = military_aviation
				}
			} 
			add_technology_researched = military_aviation
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_technology_researched = military_aviation
				NOT = {
					has_technology_researched = curtiss_seaplanes_tech
				}
			} 
			add_technology_researched = curtiss_seaplanes_tech
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_technology_researched = curtiss_seaplanes_tech
				NOT = {
					has_technology_researched = curtiss_modern_aviation_tech
				}
			} 
			add_technology_progress = { 
				progress = 8000 technology = curtiss_modern_aviation_tech
			}
		}
	}
}

#Curtiss 13: Water Airport

curtiss.13 = {
	type = country_event

    title = curtiss.13.t
		
    desc = curtiss.13.d

	flavor = curtiss.13.f

	placement = scope:curtiss_water_airport_state

	duration = 1
		
	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/curtiss_pictures/curtiss_schneider_plane_savoia.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airplane"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_aviation.dds"

	trigger = {
		has_technology_researched = curtiss_seaplanes_tech
		any_scope_state = {
			NOT = { 
				has_modifier = curtiss_water_airport_modifier
			}
			is_incorporated = yes
			any_scope_building = {
				is_building_type = building_port
				level >= 10
			}
			any_scope_building = {
				is_building_type = building_urban_center
				level >= 25
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { 
					has_modifier = curtiss_water_airport_modifier
				}
				is_incorporated = yes
				any_scope_building = {
					is_building_type = building_port
					level >= 10
				}
				any_scope_building = {
					is_building_type = building_urban_center
					level >= 25
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_water_airport_state
		}
	}

	option = { #Seaplanes are the future.
		name = curtiss.13.g
		default_option = yes
		scope:curtiss_water_airport_state = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_water_airport_modifier
			}
		}
	}
}

#Curtiss 20: Private Airline Company

curtiss.20 = {
	type = country_event

	title = curtiss.20.t

	desc = curtiss.20.d

	flavor = curtiss.20.f
	
	duration = 1

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:howard_hughes

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_aviation.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airplane"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = curtiss_private_airline
		ig:ig_industrialists = {
			save_scope_as = ig_industrialists
		}
		ig:ig_rural_folk = {
			save_scope_as = ig_rural_folk
		}
		create_character = {
			interest_group = ig_industrialists
			ideology = ideology_market_liberal
			save_scope_as = howard_hughes
			ig_leader = yes
		}
	}

	option = {	#Congratulations.
		name = curtiss.20.g
		default_option = yes
		scope:howard_hughes = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_airline_tycoon_modifier
			}
			set_variable = memento_mori_immunity
		}
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_airport
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = curtiss_thriving_aviation_modifier
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_thriving_aviation_modifier
				years = 5
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				25 = { }
				25 = {	
					trigger_event = {	
						id = curtiss.201
						days = { 300 400 }
					}
				}
				25 = {	
					trigger_event = {	
						id = curtiss.202
						days = { 300 400 }
					}
				}
				25 = {	
					trigger_event = {	
						id = curtiss.203
						days = { 300 400 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	# The future is in aviation - support the company!
		name = curtiss.20.h
		scope:howard_hughes = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_airline_tycoon_modifier
			}
			set_variable = memento_mori_immunity
		}
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_airport
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = curtiss_thriving_aviation_modifier
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_thriving_aviation_modifier
			}
		}
		ig:ig_industrialists = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_supported_airline_company_approval_modifier
				months = normal_modifier_time
			}
		}
		ig:ig_rural_folk = {	
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_supported_airline_company_disapproval_modifier
				months = normal_modifier_time
			}
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = curtiss_spent_money_on_airline_company_modifier
			multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_very_small
			years = 10
		}
		curtiss_add_1_flight_route = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				40 = {	
					trigger_event = {	
						id = curtiss.201
						days = { 300 400 }
					}
				}
				40 = {	
					trigger_event = {	
						id = curtiss.202
						days = { 300 400 }
					}
				}
				20 = {	
					trigger_event = {	
						id = curtiss.203
						days = { 300 400 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Curtiss 21: National Airline Company

curtiss.21 = {
	type = country_event

	title = curtiss.21.t

	desc = curtiss.21.d

	flavor = curtiss.21.f
	
	duration = 1

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/curtiss_pictures/curtiss_airline_imperial_1.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_aviation.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airplane"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = curtiss_state_airline
	}

	option = {	#The sky is the limit
		name = curtiss.21.g
		default_option = yes
		curtiss_add_1_flight_route = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = curtiss_spent_money_on_state_airline_company_modifier
			multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_small
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				33 = { }
				33 = {	
					trigger_event = {	
						id = curtiss.202
						days = { 300 400 }
					}
				}
				33 = {	
					trigger_event = {	
						id = curtiss.203
						days = { 300 400 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Curtiss 22: Privatization of National Airline

curtiss.22 = {
	type = country_event

	title = curtiss.22.t

	desc = curtiss.22.d

	flavor = curtiss.22.f
	
	duration = 3

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:howard_hughes

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_aviation.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airplane"

	trigger = {
		has_variable = curtiss_state_airline
		OR = { 
			has_law = law_type:law_laissez_faire
			has_law = law_type:law_interventionism
		}
		exists = ig:ig_industrialists
	}

	immediate = {
		remove_variable = curtiss_state_airline
		remove_modifier = curtiss_spent_money_on_state_airline_company_modifier
		set_variable = curtiss_private_airline
		ig:ig_industrialists = {
			save_scope_as = ig_industrialists
		}
		ig:ig_rural_folk = {
			save_scope_as = ig_rural_folk
		}
		create_character = {
			interest_group = ig_industrialists
			ideology = ideology_market_liberal
			save_scope_as = howard_hughes
			ig_leader = yes
		}
	}

	option = {	#The privatization proceeds should benefit us.
		name = curtiss.22.g
		default_option = yes
		scope:howard_hughes = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_airline_tycoon_modifier
			}
			set_variable = memento_mori_immunity
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_1_modifier
			}
			add_treasury = 50000
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_2_modifier
			}
			add_treasury = 100000
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_3_modifier
			}
			add_treasury = 150000
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_4_modifier
			}
			add_treasury = 200000
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_5_modifier
			}
			add_treasury = 300000
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_6_modifier
			}
			add_treasury = 500000
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				25 = { }
				25 = {	
					trigger_event = {	
						id = curtiss.201
						days = { 300 400 }
					}
				}
				25 = {	
					trigger_event = {	
						id = curtiss.202
						days = { 300 400 }
					}
				}
				25 = {	
					trigger_event = {	
						id = curtiss.203
						days = { 300 400 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#The company should keep the money to grow and prosper
		name = curtiss.22.h
		scope:howard_hughes = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_airline_tycoon_modifier
			}
			set_variable = memento_mori_immunity
		}
		ig:ig_industrialists = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_supported_airline_company_approval_modifier
				months = normal_modifier_time
			}
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = curtiss_no_privatization_proceeds_modifier
			years = 10
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				40 = {	
					trigger_event = {	
						id = curtiss.201
						days = { 300 400 }
					}
				}
				40 = {	
					trigger_event = {	
						id = curtiss.202
						days = { 300 400 }
					}
				}
				20 = {	
					trigger_event = {	
						id = curtiss.203
						days = { 300 400 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Curtiss 23: Nationalization of Private Airline

curtiss.23 = {
	type = country_event

	title = curtiss.23.t

	desc = curtiss.23.d

	flavor = curtiss.23.f
	
	duration = 3

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/curtiss_pictures/curtiss_airline_imperial_1.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_aviation.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airplane"

	trigger = {
		has_variable = curtiss_private_airline
		OR = { 
			has_law = law_type:law_cooperative_ownership
			has_law = law_type:law_command_economy
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		remove_variable = curtiss_private_airline
		set_variable = curtiss_state_airline
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_spent_money_on_airline_company_modifier
			}
			remove_modifier = curtiss_spent_money_on_airline_company_modifier
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_corrupting_influences_in_politics_modifier
			}
			remove_modifier = curtiss_corrupting_influences_in_politics_modifier
		}
		ig:ig_industrialists = {
			save_scope_as = ig_industrialists
		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_airline_tycoon_modifier
			}
			save_scope_as = howard_hughes
		}
	}

	option = {	#Nationalize the company in a legally sound way.
		name = curtiss.23.g
		default_option = yes
		scope:howard_hughes = {
			remove_modifier = curtiss_airline_tycoon_modifier
			remove_variable = memento_mori_immunity
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = curtiss_spent_money_on_state_airline_company_modifier
			multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_small
		}
	}

	option = {	#Those fat maggots have been eating the bacon of the people for far too long.
		name = curtiss.23.h
		scope:howard_hughes = {
			remove_modifier = curtiss_airline_tycoon_modifier
			remove_variable = memento_mori_immunity
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:howard_hughes = {
				kill_character = yes
			}
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = curtiss_spent_money_on_state_airline_company_modifier
			multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_small
		}
		ig:ig_industrialists = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_illegal_nationalization_modifier
				months = normal_modifier_time
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_1_modifier
			}
			add_treasury = 50000
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_2_modifier
			}
			add_treasury = 100000
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_3_modifier
			}
			add_treasury = 150000
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_4_modifier
			}
			add_treasury = 200000
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_5_modifier
			}
			add_treasury = 300000
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_6_modifier
			}
			add_treasury = 500000
		}
	}
}

#Curtiss 40: Transatlantic Flight (Generic)

curtiss.40 = {
	type = country_event

	title = curtiss.40.t

	desc = curtiss.40.d

	flavor = curtiss.40.f
	
	duration = 2

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/curtiss_pictures/curtiss_lindbergh_generic.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_aviation.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airplane"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = curtiss_lindbergh_happened
		random_primary_culture = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_cultural_obsession = air_travel
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = flight_addict_culture
		}
		create_character = {
			is_general = yes
			traits = { explorer brave romantic curtiss_pilot }
			birth_date = 1899.12.24
			save_scope_as = curtiss_lindbergh
		}
	}

	option = {	#Mr Lindbergh I presume.
		name = curtiss.40.g
		default_option = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			set_variable = curtiss_spirit_achievement
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = curtiss_lindbergh_modifier
			years = 10
		}
		scope:curtiss_lindbergh = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_lindbergh_character_modifier
			}
		}
		scope:flight_addict_culture = {
			add_cultural_obsession = air_travel
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					any_scope_state = {
						has_building = building_airport
					}
				}
				random = {
        			chance = 33
        			trigger_event = {
        				id = curtiss.42
        				days = { 10 30 }
					}
				}
        	}
		}
	}
}

#Curtiss 51: Helium discovered

curtiss.51 = {
	type = country_event

    title = curtiss.51.t
		
    desc = curtiss.51.d

	flavor = curtiss.51.f

	placement = scope:curtiss_helium_state

	duration = 1
		
	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/curtiss_pictures/curtiss_zeppelin_helium.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airship"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_zeppelin.dds"

	trigger = {
		any_scope_state = {
			has_building = building_oil_rig
		}
		has_technology_researched = zeppelins
		has_technology_researched = pumpjacks
		NOT = {
			has_variable = curtiss_helium_discovered
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = curtiss_helium_discovered
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_oil_rig
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_helium_state
		}
	}

	option = { #We need a strategic reserve
		name = curtiss.51.g
		default_option = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:curtiss_helium_state = {
					NOT = {
						has_modifier = curtiss_helium_reserve_modifier
					}
				}
			}
			scope:curtiss_helium_state = {
				add_modifier = {
					name = curtiss_helium_reserve_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Curtiss 53: Graf Ferdinand von Zeppelin seeks support to build an airship

curtiss.53 = {
	type = country_event

    title = curtiss.53.t
		
    desc = curtiss.53.d

	flavor = curtiss.53.f

	duration = 3

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:gaudi_new_engineer_scope

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airship"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_zeppelin.dds"

	trigger = {
		game_date >= 1890.1.1
		NOT = {
			year > 1899
		}
		NOT = {
			has_global_variable = gaudi_von_zeppelin_created
		}
		OR = {
			country_has_primary_culture = cu:south_german
			country_has_primary_culture = cu:north_german
			country_has_primary_culture = cu:united_german
			country_has_primary_culture = cu:alemannic
		}
		any_scope_state = {
			state_region = s:STATE_WURTTEMBERG #Friedrichshafen
		}
		has_technology_researched = curtiss_reconnaissance_balloon_tech
	}

	immediate = {
		create_character = {
			template = mr_ger_von_zeppelin_ferdinand_character_template

			save_scope_as = gaudi_new_engineer_scope
		}
		scope:gaudi_new_engineer_scope = {
			set_variable = gaudi_von_zeppelin_character_var
			set_variable = mr_is_engineer_var
			engineer_experience_set_up_effect = yes
			aeronautical_engineer_experience_gain_effect = {
				AMOUNT = 50
			}
			place_character_in_void = 1200
		}

		set_variable = {
			name = gaudi_new_engineer_var
			value = scope:gaudi_new_engineer_scope
		}

		set_global_variable = gaudi_von_zeppelin_created
	}

	option = { #The new Icarus. A waste of money.
		name = curtiss.53.g
		default_option = yes
		
		gaudi_remove_new_engineer_effect = yes
	}

	option = { #A formidable idea! Support him!
		name = curtiss.53.h

		add_treasury = -5000000

		gaudi_set_new_engineer_as_engineer_effect = yes

		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = curtiss.54
				years = { 2 10 }
			}
		}
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				trigger = {
					gaudi_has_engineer = no
				}
				add = 1000
			}
		}
	}
}

#Curtiss 54: Graf Ferdinand von Zeppelin

	type = country_event

    title = curtiss.54.t
		
    desc = curtiss.54.d

	flavor = curtiss.54.f

	duration = 1
		
	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/curtiss_pictures/curtiss_zeppelin_lz1.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airship"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_zeppelin.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
	}

	option = { #I knew he could do it!
		name = curtiss.54.g
		default_option = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_technology_researched = curtiss_early_aviation_tech
				}
			} 
			add_technology_researched = curtiss_early_aviation_tech
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_technology_researched = curtiss_early_aviation_tech
				NOT = {
					has_technology_researched = zeppelins
				}
			} 
			add_technology_researched = zeppelins
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_technology_researched = zeppelins
				NOT = {
					has_technology_researched = curtiss_modern_aviation_tech
				}
			} 
			add_technology_progress = { 
				progress = 8000 technology = curtiss_modern_aviation_tech
			}
		}
	}
}

#Curtiss 100: Schneider Trophy founded

curtiss.100 = {
	type = country_event

    title = curtiss.100.t
		
    desc = curtiss.100.d

	flavor = curtiss.100.f

	duration = 1

	placement = scope:curtiss_schneider_trophy_state
		
	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/curtiss_pictures/curtiss_schneider_foundation.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airplane"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_aviation.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = curtiss_schneider_trophy_host
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				is_incorporated = yes
				any_scope_building = {
					is_building_type = building_port
				}
				any_scope_building = {
					is_building_type = building_urban_center
					level >= 15
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_schneider_trophy_state
		}
		set_variable = {
            name = schneider_trophy_point
            value = 0
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = curtiss.103
				popup = yes
				days = 30
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = curtiss.108
				popup = yes
				days = 60
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = curtiss.140
				popup = yes
				days = { 65 90 }
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = curtiss.110
				popup = yes
				days = 120
			}
		}
		curtiss_create_participiants_list_schneider_effect = yes
	}

	option = { #Invite everyone to $STATE$
		name = curtiss.100.g
		scope:curtiss_schneider_trophy_state = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_schneider_trophy_state_modifier
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				curtiss_schneider_trophy_possible = yes
				NOT = {
					this = ROOT
				}
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = curtiss.101
				popup = yes
				days = 3
			}
		}
	}
}

            name = schneider_trophy_point
            value = 0
		}

			limit = {
				is_player = yes
			}
			add_treasury = -10000
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = curtiss.103
				popup = yes
				days = 30
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = curtiss.108
				popup = yes
				days = 60
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = curtiss.140
				popup = yes
				days = { 65 90 }
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = curtiss.110
				popup = yes
				days = 120
			}
		}
		curtiss_create_participiants_list_schneider_effect = yes
	}

			base = 0
		}
	}
}

#Curtiss 102: Regular Schneider Trophy

curtiss.102 = {
	type = country_event

    title = curtiss.100.t
		
    desc = curtiss.102.d

	flavor = curtiss.100.f

	duration = 1

	placement = scope:curtiss_schneider_trophy_state
		
	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/curtiss_pictures/curtiss_schneider_foundation.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airplane"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_aviation.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = curtiss_schneider_trophy_host
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						exists = c:SWI
						c:SWI = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					is_incorporated = yes
					any_scope_building = {
						is_building_type = building_port
					}
					any_scope_building = {
						is_building_type = building_urban_center
						level >= 10
					}
				}
				save_scope_as = curtiss_schneider_trophy_state
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = c:SWI
				c:SWI = ROOT
			}
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					is_incorporated = yes
					any_scope_building = {
						is_building_type = building_urban_center
						level >= 10
					}
				}
				save_scope_as = curtiss_schneider_trophy_state
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
            name = schneider_trophy_point
            value = 0
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = curtiss.103
				popup = yes
				days = 30
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = curtiss.108
				popup = yes
				days = 60
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = curtiss.140
				popup = yes
				days = { 65 90 }
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = curtiss.110
				popup = yes
				days = 120
			}
		}
		curtiss_create_participiants_list_schneider_effect = yes
	}

	option = { #Invite everyone to $STATE$
		name = curtiss.100.g
		scope:curtiss_schneider_trophy_state = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_schneider_trophy_state_modifier
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				curtiss_schneider_trophy_possible = yes
				NOT = {
					this = ROOT
				}
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = curtiss.101
				popup = yes
				days = 3
			}
		}
	}
}

#Curtiss 104: Training

curtiss.104 = {
	type = country_event

    title = curtiss.104.t
		
    desc = curtiss.104.d

	flavor = curtiss.104.f

	duration = 1
		
	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/curtiss_pictures/curtiss_schneider_test.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airplane"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_aviation.dds"

	immediate = {
	}

	option = { #Yes
		name = curtiss.103.g
		random_list = {
			30 = {
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_modifier = curtiss_pilot_school_modifier
						}
					}
					add = 10
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							any_scope_character = {
								has_trait = curtiss_pilot_ace
							}
						}
					}
					add = 15
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_modifier = curtiss_airplane_focus_modifier
						}
					}
					add = 5
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = curtiss.105
					popup = yes
					days = { 7 14 }
				}
			}
			45 = {
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							any_scope_character = {
								has_trait = curtiss_pilot_ace
							}
						}
					}
					add = 5
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_modifier = curtiss_airplane_focus_modifier
						}
					}
					add = 5
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = curtiss.106
					popup = yes
					days = { 7 14 }
				}
			}
			25 = {
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_modifier = curtiss_pilot_school_modifier
						}
					}
					add = -5
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							any_scope_character = {
								has_trait = curtiss_pilot_ace
							}
						}
					}
					add = -10
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_modifier = curtiss_airplane_focus_modifier
						}
					}
					add = -5
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = curtiss.107
					popup = yes
					days = { 7 14 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Too risky
		name = curtiss.104.h
		default_option = yes
	}
}

							has_trait = curtiss_pilot_ace
						}
					}
					kill_character = yes
				}
			}
		}

#Curtiss 108: Leading pilot

curtiss.108 = {
	type = country_event

    title = curtiss.108.t
    desc = curtiss.108.d
    flavor = curtiss.108.f

	duration = 1

    event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/curtiss_pictures/curtiss_schneider_pilot.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airplane"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_aviation.dds"

	immediate = {
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_schneider_veteran_modifier
				is_busy = no
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_schneider_pilot_1
		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = curtiss_pilot
					has_trait = curtiss_pilot_ace
				}
				NOT = {
					this = scope:curtiss_schneider_pilot_1
				}
				is_busy = no
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_schneider_pilot_2
		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = curtiss_pilot
					has_trait = curtiss_pilot_ace
				}
				NOT = {
					this = scope:curtiss_schneider_pilot_1
				}
				NOT = {
					this = scope:curtiss_schneider_pilot_2
				}
				is_busy = no
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_schneider_pilot_3
		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = curtiss_pilot
					has_trait = curtiss_pilot_ace
				}
				NOT = {
					this = scope:curtiss_schneider_pilot_1
				}
				NOT = {
					this = scope:curtiss_schneider_pilot_2
				}
				NOT = {
					this = scope:curtiss_schneider_pilot_3
				}
				is_busy = no
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_schneider_pilot_4
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = curtiss.108.g
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:curtiss_schneider_pilot_1
		}
		scope:curtiss_schneider_pilot_1 = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_schneider_pilot_modifier
			}
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = curtiss.108.h
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:curtiss_schneider_pilot_2
		}
		scope:curtiss_schneider_pilot_2 = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_schneider_pilot_modifier
			}
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = curtiss.108.i
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:curtiss_schneider_pilot_3
		}
		scope:curtiss_schneider_pilot_3 = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_schneider_pilot_modifier
			}
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = curtiss.108.j
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:curtiss_schneider_pilot_4
		}
		scope:curtiss_schneider_pilot_4 = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_schneider_pilot_modifier
			}
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = curtiss.108.k #A Newcomer
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				exists = scope:curtiss_schneider_pilot_1
			}
			NOT = {
				exists = scope:curtiss_schneider_pilot_2
			}
			NOT = {
				exists = scope:curtiss_schneider_pilot_3
			}
			NOT = {
				exists = scope:curtiss_schneider_pilot_4
			}
		}
		create_character = {
			traits = {
				curtiss_pilot
			}
			is_general = yes
			age = { 17 24 }
			save_scope_as = curtiss_new_pilot
			on_created = {
				add_modifier = {
					name = curtiss_schneider_pilot_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		trigger_event = {
			id = curtiss.104
			popup = yes
			days = { 3 10 }
		}
	}
}

#Curtiss 110: Schneider Trophy in $STATE$

curtiss.110 = {
	type = country_event

    title = curtiss.110.t
		
    desc = curtiss.110.d

	flavor = curtiss.110.f

	placement = scope:curtiss_schneider_trophy_state

	duration = 1
		
	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/curtiss_pictures/curtiss_schneider_race.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airplane"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_aviation.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		add_journal_entry = {
        	type = je_curtiss_schneider_trophy_race
        }
		###TRAINING###
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = curtiss_schneider_trophy_training_good
			}
			curtiss_add_5_schneider_trophy_point = yes 
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = curtiss_schneider_trophy_training_normal
			}
			curtiss_add_3_schneider_trophy_point = yes 
		}
		###AVIATION TECH&FOCUS###
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_technology_researched = curtiss_modern_aviation_tech
			}
			curtiss_add_2_schneider_trophy_point = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_airplane_focus_modifier
			}
			curtiss_add_1_schneider_trophy_point = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_pilot_school_modifier
			}
			curtiss_add_1_schneider_trophy_point = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_schneider_trophy_support_modifier
			}
			curtiss_add_2_schneider_trophy_point = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = curtiss_schneider_trophy_new_engine
			}
			curtiss_add_5_schneider_trophy_point = yes
		}
		###PILOTS###
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_character = {
					has_trait = curtiss_pilot
					count = 1
				}
			}
			curtiss_add_1_schneider_trophy_point = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_character = {
					has_trait = curtiss_pilot
					count = 2
				}
			}
			curtiss_add_2_schneider_trophy_point = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_character = {
					has_trait = curtiss_pilot
					count >= 3
				}
			}
			curtiss_add_3_schneider_trophy_point = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_character = {
					has_trait = curtiss_pilot_ace
				}
			}
			curtiss_add_3_schneider_trophy_point = yes
		}
		###FACTORIES###
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_state = {
					any_scope_building = {
						is_building_type = building_war_machine_industry
						level >= 5
					}
				}
			}
			curtiss_add_1_schneider_trophy_point = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_state = {
					any_scope_building = {
						is_building_type = building_war_machine_industry
						level >= 10
					}
				}
			}
			curtiss_add_1_schneider_trophy_point = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_state = {
					any_scope_building = {
						is_building_type = building_war_machine_industry
						level >= 25
					}
				}
			}
			curtiss_add_1_schneider_trophy_point = yes
		}
		###AIRPORTS###
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_state = {
					any_scope_building = {
						is_building_type = building_airport
						level >= 5
					}
				}
			}
			curtiss_add_1_schneider_trophy_point = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_state = {
					any_scope_building = {
						is_building_type = building_airport
						level >= 10
					}
				}
			}
			curtiss_add_1_schneider_trophy_point = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_state = {
					any_scope_building = {
						is_building_type = building_airport
						level >= 25
					}
				}
			}
			curtiss_add_1_schneider_trophy_point = yes
		}
		###AIRLINES###
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_1_modifier
			}
			curtiss_add_1_schneider_trophy_point = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_2_modifier
			}
			curtiss_add_2_schneider_trophy_point = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_3_modifier
			}
			curtiss_add_3_schneider_trophy_point = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_4_modifier
			}
			curtiss_add_4_schneider_trophy_point = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_5_modifier
			}
			curtiss_add_5_schneider_trophy_point = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_6_modifier
			}
			curtiss_add_6_schneider_trophy_point = yes
		}
		random_state = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_schneider_trophy_state_modifier 
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_schneider_trophy_state
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = curtiss_schneider_trophy_host
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_schneider_trophy_host
		}
	}

	option = { #Let's have fun
		name = curtiss.110.g
		default_option = yes
		remove_variable = curtiss_schneider_trophy_training_good
		remove_variable = curtiss_schneider_trophy_training_normal
		remove_variable = curtiss_schneider_trophy_new_engine
	}
}

#Curtiss 111: Schneider Trophy Victory

curtiss.111 = {
	type = country_event

    title = curtiss.111.t
		
    desc = curtiss.111.d

	flavor = curtiss.111.f

	duration = 1
		
	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/curtiss_pictures/curtiss_schneider_victory.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airplane"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_aviation.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = curtiss_last_trophy_winner_var
			}
			remove_variable = curtiss_last_trophy_winner_var
		}
		set_variable = curtiss_last_trophy_winner_var
		set_global_variable = curtiss_schneider_trophy_race_end
		set_variable = {
			name = curtiss_schneider_trophy_recent_winner
			days = 60
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = curtiss_schneider_trophy_break_modifier
			days = 365
		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_schneider_pilot_modifier
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = curtiss_schneider_veteran_modifier
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_schneider_veteran_modifier
			} 
		}
		#Used to display victories in GUI
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_variable = curtiss_schneider_trophy_victories_var } }
			set_variable = {
				name = curtiss_schneider_trophy_victories_var
				value = 1
			}
		}
		else = {
			change_variable = {
				name = curtiss_schneider_trophy_victories_var
				add = 1
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Victory!
		name = curtiss.111.g
		default_option = yes
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_variable = curtiss_schneider_trophy_member
					has_variable = curtiss_schneider_trophy_host
				}
				NOT = {
					this = ROOT
				}
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = curtiss.112
				popup = yes
				days = 3
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_schneider_trophy_2_win_modifier
			}
			remove_modifier = curtiss_schneider_trophy_2_win_modifier
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_the_schneider_trophy_modifier
			}
			random_scope_character = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = curtiss_schneider_pilot_modifier
				}
				add_modifier = curtiss_schneider_winner_modifier
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				trigger_event = {
					id = curtiss.113
					popup = yes
					days = 3
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_schneider_trophy_1_win_modifier
			}
			remove_modifier = curtiss_schneider_trophy_1_win_modifier
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_schneider_trophy_2_win_modifier
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = curtiss_schneider_trophy_1_win_modifier
				}
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = curtiss_schneider_trophy_2_win_modifier
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_schneider_trophy_1_win_modifier
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		remove_variable = curtiss_schneider_trophy_member
		remove_variable = curtiss_schneider_trophy_host
		remove_modifier = curtiss_schneider_trophy_support_modifier
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_schneider_pilot_modifier
			}
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = no
			remove_modifier = curtiss_schneider_pilot_modifier
		}
		random_state = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_schneider_trophy_state_modifier
			}
			remove_modifier = curtiss_schneider_trophy_state_modifier
		}
		curtiss_remove_participiants_list_schneider_effect = yes
	}
}

#Curtiss 112: Schneider Trophy Lost

curtiss.112 = {
	type = country_event

    title = curtiss.112.t
		
    desc = curtiss.112.d

	flavor = curtiss.112.f

	duration = 1
		
	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/curtiss_pictures/curtiss_schneider_lost.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airplane"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_aviation.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = curtiss_schneider_trophy_recent_winner
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_schneider_trophy_recent_winner
		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_schneider_pilot_modifier
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = curtiss_schneider_veteran_modifier
				}
			}
			add_modifier = curtiss_schneider_veteran_modifier
		}
	}

	option = { #Disappointing
		name = curtiss.112.g
		default_option = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_schneider_trophy_1_win_modifier
			}
			remove_modifier = curtiss_schneider_trophy_1_win_modifier
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_schneider_trophy_2_win_modifier
			}
			remove_modifier = curtiss_schneider_trophy_2_win_modifier
		}
	}

	after = {
		remove_variable = curtiss_schneider_trophy_member
		remove_variable = curtiss_schneider_trophy_host
		remove_modifier = curtiss_schneider_trophy_support_modifier
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_schneider_pilot_modifier
			}
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = no
			remove_modifier = curtiss_schneider_pilot_modifier
		}
	}
}

#Curtiss 124: Maximum Speed

curtiss.124 = {
	type = country_event

    title = curtiss.124.t
		
    desc = curtiss.124.d

	flavor = curtiss.124.f

	duration = 1

	placement = scope:curtiss_schneider_trophy_state
		
	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/curtiss_pictures/curtiss_schneider_plane_curtiss.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airplane"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_aviation.dds"
	
	cooldown = { 
		months = 1
	}

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		random_state = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_schneider_trophy_state_modifier 
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_schneider_trophy_state
		}
	}

	option = { #Full Power!
		name = curtiss.124.g
		curtiss_add_2_schneider_trophy_point = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_technology_researched = curtiss_modern_aviation_tech
			}
			curtiss_add_2_schneider_trophy_point = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_character = {
					has_modifier = curtiss_schneider_pilot_modifier
					has_trait = curtiss_pilot_ace
				}
			}
			curtiss_add_1_schneider_trophy_point = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_character = {
					has_modifier = curtiss_schneider_pilot_modifier
					has_modifier = curtiss_schneider_veteran_modifier
				}
			}
			curtiss_add_1_schneider_trophy_point = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_character = {
					has_modifier = curtiss_schneider_pilot_modifier
					OR = {
						has_trait = brave
						has_trait = reckless
						has_trait = innovative
						has_trait = ambitious
						has_trait = direct
					}
				}
			}
			curtiss_add_1_schneider_trophy_point = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_airplane_focus_modifier
			}
			curtiss_add_1_schneider_trophy_point = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_schneider_trophy_support_modifier
			}
			curtiss_add_1_schneider_trophy_point = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = gaudi_engineer_var
			}
			curtiss_add_1_schneider_trophy_point = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				gaudi_has_aeronautical_engineer_trigger = yes
			}
			curtiss_add_1_schneider_trophy_point = yes
		}
	}

	after = {
	}
}

#Curtiss 126: Fog

curtiss.126 = {

    title = curtiss.126.t

	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airplane"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_aviation.dds"
	
	cooldown = { 
		months = 1
	}

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		random_state = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_schneider_trophy_state_modifier 
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_schneider_trophy_state
		}
	}

	option = { #Our pilot will find his way
		name = curtiss.126.g
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_character = {
					has_modifier = curtiss_schneider_pilot_modifier
					has_trait = curtiss_pilot_ace
				}
			}
			curtiss_add_1_schneider_trophy_point = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_character = {
					has_modifier = curtiss_schneider_pilot_modifier
					has_modifier = curtiss_schneider_veteran_modifier
				}
			}
			curtiss_add_1_schneider_trophy_point = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_character = {
					has_modifier = curtiss_schneider_pilot_modifier
					OR = {
						has_trait = innovative
						has_trait = persistent
						has_trait = tactful
						has_trait = meticulous
						has_trait = cautious
						has_trait = brave
					}
				}
			}
			curtiss_add_2_schneider_trophy_point = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_pilot_school_modifier
			}
			curtiss_add_1_schneider_trophy_point = yes
		}
	}

	after = {
	}
}

		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/curtiss_pictures/curtiss_schneider_plane_supermarine.dds"
	}

	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airplane"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_aviation.dds"
	
	cooldown = { 
		months = 2
	}

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			any_scope_character = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_schneider_pilot_modifier
				has_trait = curtiss_pilot_ace
			}
			any_scope_character = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_schneider_pilot_modifier
				has_modifier = curtiss_schneider_veteran_modifier
			}
		}
		any_scope_character = {
			has_modifier = curtiss_schneider_pilot_modifier
			OR = {
				has_trait = innovative
				has_trait = persistent
				has_trait = ambitious
				has_trait = brave
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_state = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_schneider_trophy_state_modifier 
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_schneider_trophy_state
		}
	}

	option = { #Excellent!
		name = curtiss.127.g
		curtiss_add_4_schneider_trophy_point = yes
	}

	after = {
	}
}

curtiss.135 = {
	type = country_event

    title = curtiss.135.t
    desc = curtiss.135.d
    flavor = curtiss.135.f

	duration = 1

    event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/curtiss_pictures/curtiss_schneider_engine.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airplane"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_aviation.dds"

	cooldown = { 
		months = 6
	}

	immediate = {

			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_schneider_trophy_state_modifier

			save_scope_as = curtiss_schneider_trophy_state
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				curtiss_schneider_can_be_sabotaged = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_schneider_sabotage_country_1
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				curtiss_schneider_can_be_sabotaged = yes
				NOT = {
					this = scope:curtiss_schneider_sabotage_country_1
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_schneider_sabotage_country_2
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				curtiss_schneider_can_be_sabotaged = yes
				NOT = {
					this = scope:curtiss_schneider_sabotage_country_1
				}
				NOT = {
					this = scope:curtiss_schneider_sabotage_country_2
				}

		}

				NOT = {

	placement = scope:curtiss_schneider_trophy_state

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/curtiss_pictures/curtiss_schneider_engine.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airplane"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_aviation.dds"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		random_state = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_schneider_trophy_state_modifier 
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_schneider_trophy_state
		}
	}

	option = { #Smells like sabotage ...
		name = curtiss.136.g
		curtiss_sub_5_schneider_trophy_point = yes
	}

	after = {
	}
}

#Curtiss 140: [Aeronautical Engineer] constructs new engine

	type = country_event

    title = curtiss.140.t
		
    desc = curtiss.140.d

	flavor = curtiss.140.f

	duration = 1

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:gaudi_engineer_scope

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airplane"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_aviation.dds"

	trigger = {
		gaudi_has_aeronautical_engineer_trigger = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		var:gaudi_engineer_var = {
			save_scope_as = gaudi_engineer_scope
		}
	}

	option = { #A technical wonder!
		name = curtiss.140.g
		default_option = yes
		
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = curtiss_schneider_trophy_new_engine_tt
			set_variable = curtiss_schneider_trophy_new_engine
		}
	}
}

######AIRLINES######

#Curtiss 201: Airline invests in airport

curtiss.201 = {
	type = country_event

	title = curtiss.201.t

	desc = curtiss.201.d

	flavor = curtiss.201.f
	
	duration = 3

	placement = scope:curtiss_new_airport_state

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/curtiss_pictures/curtiss_airline_klm_1.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_aviation.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airplane"

	trigger = {
		any_scope_state = {
			is_incorporated = yes
			any_scope_building = {
				is_building_type = building_urban_center
				level >= 15
			}
			NOT = {
				has_building = building_airport
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		ig:ig_industrialists = {
			save_scope_as = ig_industrialists
		}
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				is_incorporated = yes
				any_scope_building = {
					is_building_type = building_urban_center
					level >= 15
				}
				NOT = {
					has_building = building_airport
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_new_airport_state
		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_airline_tycoon_modifier
			}
			save_scope_as = howard_hughes
		}
	}

	option = {	#Build a new airport.
		name = curtiss.201.g
		default_option = yes
		curtiss_add_1_flight_route = yes
		scope:curtiss_new_airport_state = {
			create_building = {
				building = "building_airport"
			}
			activate_building = {
				building = "building_airport"
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_thriving_aviation_modifier
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Expand the airline, but invest the capital elsewhere.
		name = curtiss.201.h
		curtiss_add_1_flight_route = yes
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_airport
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = curtiss_expanded_airline_modifier
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_expanded_airline_modifier
				years = 10
			}
		}
	}
}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airplane"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_airline_tycoon_modifier
			}
			save_scope_as = howard_hughes
		}
	}

	option = {	#Disappointing.
		name = curtiss.203.g
		default_option = yes
	}

	option = {	#Send one of our pilots to advertise the airline.
		name = curtiss.203.h
		trigger = {
			curtiss_has_active_pilot = yes 
		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = curtiss_pilot
					has_trait = curtiss_pilot_ace
				}
			}
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_airline_advertising_modifier
				days = 550
			}
		}
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_airport
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = curtiss_expanded_airline_modifier
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_expanded_airline_modifier
				years = 10
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = curtiss.204
				days = 551
			}
		}
	}
}

#Curtiss 211: New Flight Route to foreign Airport

curtiss.211 = {
	type = country_event

	title = curtiss.211.t

	desc = curtiss.211.d

	flavor = curtiss.211.f
	
	duration = 3

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/curtiss_pictures/curtiss_airline_FRA.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_aviation.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airplane"

	trigger = {
		curtiss_has_airline = yes
		any_country = {
			has_diplomatic_pact = {
				who = ROOT
				type = airspace_convention
			}
			any_scope_state = {
				has_building = building_airport
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = curtiss_foreign_airline_modifier
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_modifier = curtiss_new_frontiers_modifier
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_diplomatic_pact = {
					who = ROOT
					type = airspace_convention
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_airline_country
		}
	}

	option = {	#Hopefully this investment is worth it.
		name = curtiss.211.g
		default_option = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = curtiss_new_frontiers_modifier
			years = 3
		}
		scope:curtiss_airline_country = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = curtiss.212
			}
		}
	}
}

#Curtiss 215: Colonial Goods

curtiss.215 = {
	type = country_event

	title = curtiss.215.t

	desc = curtiss.215.d

	flavor = curtiss.215.f
	
	duration = 3

	placement = scope:curtiss_airport_state

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/curtiss_pictures/curtiss_airline_usa_5.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_aviation.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airplane"

	cooldown = { 
		years = 5
	}

	trigger = {
		curtiss_has_airline = yes
		any_scope_state = {
			is_incorporated = no
			state_in_africa = yes
			any_scope_building = {
				is_building_type = building_urban_center
				level >= 3
			}
			NOT = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_colonial_airport_modifier
			}
		}
		any_scope_state = {
			is_incorporated = yes
			state_in_africa = no
			any_scope_building = {
				is_building_type = building_airport
				level >= 3
			}
			NOT = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_colonial_goods_modifier
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				is_incorporated = no
				state_in_africa = yes
				any_scope_building = {
					is_building_type = building_urban_center
					level >= 3
				}
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = curtiss_colonial_airport_modifier
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_airport_state
		}
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				is_incorporated = yes
				state_in_africa = no
				any_scope_building = {
					is_building_type = building_airport
					level >= 3
				}
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = curtiss_colonial_goods_modifier
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_colonial_goods_state
		}
	}

	option = {	#Even the most remote areas of the world are linked by aviation to the heartland.
		name = curtiss.215.g
		default_option = yes
		scope:curtiss_airport_state = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_colonial_airport_modifier
			}
		}
		scope:curtiss_colonial_goods_state = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_colonial_goods_modifier
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
	}
}

#Curtiss 218: A Pilot for advertising?

curtiss.218 = {
	type = country_event

	title = curtiss.218.t

	desc = curtiss.218.d

	flavor = curtiss.218.f
	
	duration = 1

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/curtiss_pictures/curtiss_airline_usa_3.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_aviation.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airplane"

	cooldown = { 
		years = 4
	}

	trigger = {
		curtiss_has_active_pilot = yes
		curtiss_has_airline = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_airline_tycoon_modifier
			}
			save_scope_as = howard_hughes
		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = curtiss_pilot
					has_trait = curtiss_pilot_ace
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_pilot
		}
	}

	option = {	#Sure!
		name = curtiss.218.g
		default_option = yes
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = curtiss_pilot
					has_trait = curtiss_pilot_ace
				}
			}
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_airline_advertising_modifier
				days = 550
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_state = {
					has_building = building_airport
					NOT = {
						has_modifier = curtiss_expanded_airline_modifier
					}
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_expanded_airline_modifier
				years = 5
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = curtiss.204
				days = 551
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#We cannot do without him, but we help in other ways.
		name = curtiss.218.h
		add_modifier = {
			name = curtiss_spent_additional_money_on_airline_company_modifier
			multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_very_small
			days = 550
		}
	}

	option = {	#Unfortunately, our hands are tied.
		name = curtiss.218.i
		curtiss_sub_1_flight_route = yes
	}

	after = {
	}
}

				name = curtiss_investment_new_aircraft_modifier
				multiplier = money_amount_multiplier_very_small
				years = 2
			}
		}
	}
	option = {	#We can't afford that.
		name = curtiss.219.h
		trigger = {
			has_variable = curtiss_state_airline
		}
	}
}

		has_variable = curtiss_private_airline
		curtiss_subsidizes_airline = no
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_airline_tycoon_modifier
			}
			save_scope_as = howard_hughes
		}
		ig:ig_industrialists = {
			save_scope_as = ig_industrialists
		}
		ig:ig_trade_unions = {
			save_scope_as = ig_trade_unions
		}
	}

	option = {	#It's called free market for reasons.
		name = curtiss.222.g
		default_option = yes
		curtiss_sub_1_flight_route = yes
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_modifier = curtiss_thriving_aviation_modifier
					has_modifier = curtiss_expanded_airline_modifier
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_airline_in_crisis_modifier
				years = 3
			}
		}
		ig:ig_trade_unions = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_not_saved_airline_from_crisis_modifier
				years = 3
			}
		}
		scope:howard_hughes = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_airline_tycoon_in_trouble_modifier
				years = 3
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#This company is of national importance!

			years = 3
		}
		ig:ig_industrialists = {
			add_modifier = {

				years = 3
			}
		}
	}
}

curtiss.224 = {

		var:curtiss_flight_route >= 9
		NOT = {
			any_scope_character = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_airline_tycoon_powerful_modifier
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {

			}

			}

#Curtiss 226: Competing airline

curtiss.226 = {
	type = country_event

	title = curtiss.226.t

	desc = curtiss.226.d

	flavor = curtiss.226.f
	
	duration = 3

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/curtiss_pictures/curtiss_airline_imperial_2.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_aviation.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airplane"

	trigger = {
		curtiss_has_airline = yes
		any_country = {
			has_diplomatic_pact = {
				who = ROOT
				type = rivalry
			}
			curtiss_has_airline = yes
		}
		any_country = {
			has_diplomatic_pact = {
				who = ROOT
				type = airspace_convention
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_modifier = curtiss_rival_airline_modifier
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_diplomatic_pact = {
					who = ROOT
					type = rivalry
				}
				curtiss_has_airline = yes
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_rival_airline_country
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_diplomatic_pact = {
					who = ROOT
					type = airspace_convention
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_third_country
		}
	}

	option = {	#We don't interfere
		name = curtiss.226.g
		default_option = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = curtiss_rival_airline_modifier
			years = 2
		}
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_airport
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = curtiss_airline_in_crisis_modifier
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_airline_in_crisis_modifier
				years = 2
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Attempt diplomatic intervention in THIRD COUNTRY.
		name = curtiss.226.h
		add_modifier = {
			name = curtiss_diplomatic_airline_intervention_modifier
			years = 2
		}
	}
}

#Curtiss 227: Airline Tycoon in trouble

curtiss.227 = {
	type = country_event

	title = curtiss.227.t

	desc = curtiss.227.d

	flavor = curtiss.227.f
	
	duration = 3

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:howard_hughes

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_aviation.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airplane"

	trigger = {
		has_variable = curtiss_private_airline
		any_scope_character = {
			has_modifier = curtiss_airline_tycoon_modifier
			is_ruler = no
		}
		NOT = {
			has_variable = curtiss_building_spruce_goose
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_airline_tycoon_modifier
			}
			save_scope_as = howard_hughes
		}
		ig:ig_industrialists = {
			save_scope_as = ig_industrialists
		}
	}

	option = {	#He should step back.
		name = curtiss.224.g
		default_option = yes
		scope:howard_hughes = {
			remove_modifier = curtiss_airline_tycoon_modifier
			remove_variable = memento_mori_immunity
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:howard_hughes = {
				kill_character = yes
			}
		}
		ig:ig_industrialists = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_disapproves_airline_tycoon_modifier
				years = 5
			}
		}
		create_character = {
			interest_group = ig_industrialists
			ideology = ideology_market_liberal
			ig_leader = yes
		}
	}

	option = {	#$HOWARD HUGHES$ will master this minor crisis.
		name = curtiss.224.h
		every_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_thriving_aviation_modifier
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_airline_in_crisis_modifier
				years = 1
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		random_interest_group = {
			limit = {
				is_interest_group_type = ig_industrialists
			}
			leader = {
				add_modifier = {
					name = curtiss_airline_tycoon_modifier
				}
				set_variable = memento_mori_immunity
			}
		}
	}
}

			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_variable = curtiss_hughes_offered_industry
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = curtiss_hughes_offered_industry
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_modifier = curtiss_thriving_aviation_modifier
					has_modifier = curtiss_expanded_airline_modifier

				NOT = {

		ig:ig_industrialists = {
			save_scope_as = ig_industrialists
		}
	}

	option = {	#A great day for aviation!

		}

				name = curtiss_airplane_constructor_modifier

#Curtiss 251: Lost Pilot [Shangri-La Opening]

curtiss.251 = {
	type = country_event

	title = curtiss.251.t

	desc = curtiss.251.d

	flavor = curtiss.251.f
	
	duration = 3

	placement = scope:curtiss_himalaya

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:curtiss_conway_scope

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_aviation.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_game_rule = lepsius_only_historical_rule
		}
		is_player = yes
		curtiss_has_airline = yes
		curtiss_has_pilot = yes
		any_scope_building = {
			is_building_type = building_lepsius_archaeological_museum
		}
		NOT = {
			has_variable = curtiss_shangri_la_opening
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = curtiss_shangri_la_opening
		random_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_HIMALAYAS
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_himalaya
		}
		create_conway_effect = yes
		set_variable = {
            name = curtiss_shangrila_progress
            value = 0
		}
	}

	option = {	#We should outfit an expedition
		name = curtiss.251.g
		default_option = yes
		set_variable = curtiss_search_for_conway
	}

	option = {	#No
		name = curtiss.251.h
	}
}

#Curtiss 252: Conway expedition leader

curtiss.252 = {
	type = country_event

    title = curtiss.252.t
    desc = curtiss.252.d
    flavor = curtiss.252.f

    event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/curtiss_pictures/curtiss_shangrila_legend.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_aviation.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

    duration = 3

	immediate = {
		var:curtiss_conway_var = {
			save_scope_as = curtiss_conway_scope
		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = curtiss_pilot
					has_trait = curtiss_pilot_ace
				}
				is_busy = no
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_expedition_leader_1
		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = curtiss_pilot
					has_trait = curtiss_pilot_ace
				}
				NOT = {
					this = scope:curtiss_expedition_leader_1
				}
				is_busy = no
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_expedition_leader_2
		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = curtiss_pilot
					has_trait = curtiss_pilot_ace
				}
				NOT = {
					this = scope:curtiss_expedition_leader_1
				}
				NOT = {
					this = scope:curtiss_expedition_leader_2
				}
				is_busy = no
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_expedition_leader_3
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = curtiss.252.g
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:curtiss_expedition_leader_1
		}
		scope:curtiss_expedition_leader_1 = {
			set_variable = curtiss_shangrila_leader_var
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = curtiss.252.h
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:curtiss_expedition_leader_2
		}
		scope:curtiss_expedition_leader_2 = {
			set_variable = curtiss_shangrila_leader_var
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = curtiss.252.i
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:curtiss_expedition_leader_3
		}
		scope:curtiss_expedition_leader_3 = {
			set_variable = curtiss_shangrila_leader_var
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
		}
	}

	after = {
		trigger_event = {
			id = curtiss.253
			days = { 3 7 }
		}
	}
}

	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_aviation.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

    duration = 3

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		var:curtiss_conway_var = {
			save_scope_as = curtiss_conway_scope
		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = curtiss_shangrila_leader_var
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_shangrila_leader
		}
		random_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_KASHMIR
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_ladakh
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = curtiss.270.g #A Kora ...
		set_variable = curtiss_shangrila_advice
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = curtiss.261

			}
		}
	}
}

#Curtiss 271: Lhasa

curtiss.271 = {
	type = country_event

    title = curtiss.271.t
    desc = curtiss.271.d
    flavor = curtiss.271.f

	placement = scope:curtiss_lhasa

    event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/curtiss_pictures/curtiss_shangrila_lhasa.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_aviation.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

    duration = 3

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = curtiss_road_to_shangrila
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		var:curtiss_conway_var = {
			save_scope_as = curtiss_conway_scope
		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = curtiss_shangrila_leader_var
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_shangrila_leader

			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_LHASA
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_lhasa
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = curtiss.271.g #Visit the Lama
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_variable = curtiss_shangrila_second_artifact
			}
		}
		default_option = yes

				id = curtiss.272

			}
		}

#Curtiss 283: Lost in the Wilderness

	type = country_event

    desc = curtiss.283.d

		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/curtiss_pictures/curtiss_shangrila_lost.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_aviation.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

    duration = 3

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		var:curtiss_conway_var = {
			save_scope_as = curtiss_conway_scope
		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = curtiss_shangrila_leader_var
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_shangrila_leader
		}
		random_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_NGARI
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_ngari
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = curtiss.283.g #Just narrowly escaped death.
		default_option = yes
		scope:curtiss_shangrila_leader = {
			add_trait = wounded
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_shangrila_near_death_modifier
				days = 90
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = curtiss.254
				days = 90
				popup = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

#Curtiss 296: Decision

curtiss.296 = {
	type = country_event

	title = curtiss.296.t

	desc = curtiss.296.d

	flavor = curtiss.296.f

	placement = scope:curtiss_himalaya

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:curtiss_conway_scope

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_aviation.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		var:curtiss_conway_var = {
			save_scope_as = curtiss_conway_scope
		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = curtiss_shangrila_leader_var
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_shangrila_leader
		}
		random_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_HIMALAYAS
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_himalaya
		}
		set_variable = curtiss_lost_horizon_achievement
	}

	option = {	#This place should remain secret. I just want to learn
		name = curtiss.296.g
		default_option = yes
		scope:curtiss_shangrila_leader = {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = no
			add_trait = persistent
			add_trait = tactful
			add_trait = meticulous
			add_trait = charismatic
			add_trait = brave
			add_trait = pious
			add_trait = explorer
			add_trait = elgar_composer
			add_trait = lepsius_archaeologist
			add_trait = verrier_astronomer
			remove_trait = arrogant
			remove_trait = bigoted
			remove_trait = reckless
			remove_trait = ambitious
			remove_trait = imperious
			remove_trait = wrathful
			remove_trait = cruel
			remove_trait = hedonist
			remove_trait = alcoholic
			remove_trait = opium_addiction
			remove_trait = cocaine_addiction
			remove_trait = wounded
			remove_trait = psychological_affliction
			remove_trait = expensive_tastes
		}
	}

	option = {	#This place should be protected. I will stay.
		name = curtiss.296.h
		create_country = {
			tag = SLA
			province = p:x2D753F
			origin = ROOT
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:curtiss_shangrila_leader = {
				set_character_busy_and_immortal = no
				add_trait = persistent
				add_trait = tactful
				add_trait = meticulous
				add_trait = charismatic

				remove_trait = bigoted
				remove_trait = reckless
				remove_trait = ambitious
				remove_trait = imperious
				remove_trait = wrathful
				remove_trait = cruel
				remove_trait = hedonist
				remove_trait = alcoholic

				remove_trait = cocaine_addiction
				remove_trait = cancer
				remove_trait = grifter
				remove_trait = scarred
				remove_trait = senile
				remove_trait = syphilis
				remove_trait = shellshocked
				remove_trait = wounded
				remove_trait = psychological_affliction
				remove_trait = expensive_tastes
				remove_trait = kidney_stones
				remove_trait = beetle_ear
			}
		}
		scope:curtiss_shangrila_leader = {
			transfer_character = c:SLA
		}
		set_variable = curtiss_shangrila_padron
		hidden_effect = {
			c:SLA = {
				trigger_event = {
					id = curtiss.297
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#This place will be ours. In the name of COUNTRY!
		name = curtiss.296.i
		change_infamy = 10
		scope:curtiss_shangrila_leader = {
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = no
			remove_trait = persistent
			remove_trait = tactful
			remove_trait = meticulous
			remove_trait = charismatic
			remove_trait = brave
			remove_trait = pious
			add_trait = arrogant
			add_trait = bigoted
			add_trait = reckless

		curtiss_add_artifacts_of_shangrila = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = curtiss_shangrila_secrets_modifier
			years = 10
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = curtiss.298
				days = { 3 7 }
			}
		}
	}

		activate_law = law_type:law_multicultural
		activate_law = law_type:law_no_colonial_affairs
		activate_law = law_type:law_autocracy
		activate_law = law_type:law_agrarianism
		activate_law = law_type:law_religious_schools
		activate_law = law_type:law_protected_speech
		activate_law = law_type:law_theocracy
		activate_law = law_type:law_charitable_health_system
		activate_law = law_type:law_guaranteed_liberties
		activate_law = law_type:law_worker_protections
		activate_law = law_type:law_closed_borders
		activate_law = law_type:law_local_police
		activate_law = law_type:law_womens_suffrage
		activate_law = law_type:law_slavery_banned
		activate_law = law_type:law_land_based_taxation
		activate_law = law_type:law_isolationism
		activate_law = law_type:law_right_of_assembly
		activate_law = law_type:law_poor_laws

		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = curtiss_shangrila_padron
			}
			create_diplomatic_pact = {
				country = c:SLA
				type = puppet
			}
		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = curtiss_shangrila_leader_var
			}
			set_character_as_ruler = yes
		}
	}
}

	}

		var:curtiss_conway_var = {
			save_scope_as = curtiss_conway_scope
		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = curtiss_shangrila_leader_var
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_shangrila_leader
		}
		random_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_HIMALAYAS
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_himalaya
		}
		set_variable = curtiss_lost_horizon_achievement
	}

	option = {	#
		name = curtiss.298.g
		default_option = yes
		scope:curtiss_shangrila_leader = {
			kill_character = yes
		}
	}
}

	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airplane"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_airline_tycoon_modifier
			}

		}
	}

        }

			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#This is madness.
		name = curtiss.500.h
	}
}
