#Curtiss 505: The Greatest Day in History

curtiss.505 = {
	type = country_event

	title = curtiss.505.t

	desc = curtiss.505.d

	flavor = curtiss.505.f
	
	duration = 2

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/curtiss_pictures/curtiss_hercules_5.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_aviation.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airplane"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_airline_tycoon_modifier
			}
			save_scope_as = howard_hughes
		}
	}

	option = {	#Mr. Hughes will fly it
		name = curtiss.505.g
		default_option = yes
		set_variable = curtiss_sc_hughes
	}

	option = {	#A known pilot will fly it
		name = curtiss.505.h
		set_variable = curtiss_sc_pilot
	}

	option = {	#Only test pilot
		name = curtiss.505.i
		set_variable = curtiss_sc_test
	}

	after = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:curtiss_spruce_goose_errors = 0
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = curtiss.506
				days = 3
				popup = yes 
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:curtiss_spruce_goose_errors >= 1
				NOT = {
					var:curtiss_spruce_goose_errors >= 3
				}
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = curtiss.507
				days = 3
				popup = yes 
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:curtiss_spruce_goose_errors >= 3
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = curtiss.508
				days = 3
				popup = yes 
			}
		}
	}
}

#Curtiss 506: It flies! It really flies!

curtiss.506 = {
	type = country_event

	title = curtiss.506.t

	desc = curtiss.506.d

	flavor = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = curtiss_sc_hughes
			}
			desc = curtiss.506.f_hughes
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = curtiss_sc_pilot
			}
			desc = curtiss.506.f_pilot
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = curtiss_sc_test
			}
			desc = curtiss.506.f_test
		}
	}
	
	duration = 2

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/curtiss_pictures/curtiss_hercules_6.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_aviation.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airplane"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = curtiss_aviator_achievement
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_airline_tycoon_modifier
			}
			save_scope_as = howard_hughes
		}
	}

	option = {	#This is surprising...in a very positive way!
		name = curtiss.506.g
		default_option = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = curtiss_sc_hughes
			}
			scope:howard_hughes = {
				add_modifier = {
					name = curtiss_the_aviator_modifier
				}
			}
			every_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_building = building_airport
						has_building = building_war_machine_industry
					}
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = curtiss_airplane_revolution_modifier
					years = 10
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_spruce_goose_modifier
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = curtiss_sc_pilot
			}
			every_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_building = building_airport
						has_building = building_war_machine_industry
					}
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = curtiss_airplane_revolution_modifier
					years = 5
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_spruce_goose_modifier
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = curtiss_sc_test
			}
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_building = building_airport
						has_building = building_war_machine_industry
					}
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = curtiss_airplane_revolution_modifier
					years = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		default_option = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = curtiss_sc_hughes
			}
			scope:howard_hughes = {
				remove_modifier = curtiss_airline_tycoon_modifier
				remove_variable = memento_mori_immunity
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				scope:howard_hughes = {
					kill_character = yes
				}
			}
			create_character = {
				interest_group = ig_industrialists
				ideology = ideology_market_liberal
				ig_leader = yes
			}
			every_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = curtiss_thriving_aviation_modifier
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = curtiss_airline_in_crisis_modifier
					years = 5
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = curtiss_sc_pilot
			}
			scope:howard_hughes = {
				remove_modifier = curtiss_airline_tycoon_modifier
				remove_variable = memento_mori_immunity
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				scope:howard_hughes = {
					kill_character = yes
				}
			}
			create_character = {
				interest_group = ig_industrialists
				ideology = ideology_market_liberal
				ig_leader = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = curtiss_sc_test
			}
			scope:howard_hughes = {
				add_modifier = {
					name = curtiss_awkwardly_silent_tycoon_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		random_interest_group = {
			limit = {
				is_interest_group_type = ig_industrialists
			}
			leader = {
				add_modifier = {
					name = curtiss_airline_tycoon_modifier
				}
				set_variable = memento_mori_immunity
			}
		}
	}
}

#Curtiss 508: A Nightmare

curtiss.508 = {
	type = country_event

	title = curtiss.508.t

	desc = curtiss.508.d

	flavor = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = curtiss_sc_hughes
			}
			desc = curtiss.508.f_hughes
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = curtiss_sc_pilot
			}
			desc = curtiss.508.f_pilot
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = curtiss_sc_test
			}
			desc = curtiss.508.f_test
		}
	}
	
	duration = 2

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/curtiss_pictures/curtiss_hercules_8.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_aviation.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airplane"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_airline_tycoon_modifier
			}
			save_scope_as = howard_hughes
		}
	}

	option = {	#This is the blackest day in aviation history.
		name = curtiss.508.g
		default_option = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = curtiss_sc_hughes
			}
			scope:howard_hughes = {
				kill_character = yes
			}
			remove_variable = curtiss_private_airline
			remove_modifier = curtiss_airline_level_6_modifier
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_spruce_goose_desaster_modifier
			}
			set_variable = {
            	name = curtiss_flight_route
            	value = 0
			}
			every_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					has_building = building_airport
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = curtiss_airline_in_crisis_modifier
					years = 10
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = curtiss_sc_pilot
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_spruce_goose_desaster_modifier
			}
			scope:howard_hughes = {
				remove_modifier = curtiss_airline_tycoon_modifier
				remove_variable = memento_mori_immunity
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				scope:howard_hughes = {
					kill_character = yes
				}
			}
			create_character = {
				interest_group = ig_industrialists
				ideology = ideology_market_liberal
				ig_leader = yes
			}
			every_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_modifier = curtiss_thriving_aviation_modifier
						has_modifier = curtiss_expanded_airline_modifier
					}
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = curtiss_airline_in_crisis_modifier
					years = 5
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = curtiss_sc_test
			}
			scope:howard_hughes = {
				remove_modifier = curtiss_airline_tycoon_modifier
				remove_variable = memento_mori_immunity
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				scope:howard_hughes = {
					kill_character = yes
				}
			}
			create_character = {
				interest_group = ig_industrialists
				ideology = ideology_market_liberal
				ig_leader = yes
			}
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = curtiss_thriving_aviation_modifier
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = curtiss_airline_in_crisis_modifier
					years = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		random_interest_group = {
			limit = {
				is_interest_group_type = ig_industrialists
			}
			leader = {
				add_modifier = {
					name = curtiss_airline_tycoon_modifier
				}
				set_variable = memento_mori_immunity
			}
		}
	}
}

		}

					is_building_type = building_war_machine_industry

				name = curtiss_zeppelin_wharf_modifier
			}

#Curtiss 511: $COUNTRY$'s Maiden Voyage

curtiss.511 = {
	type = country_event

	title = curtiss.511.t

	desc = curtiss.511.d

	flavor = curtiss.511.f
	
	duration = 2

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/curtiss_pictures/curtiss_zeppelin_city.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_zeppelin.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airship"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		remove_modifier = curtiss_hindenburg_build_modifier
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				has_diplomatic_pact = {
					who = ROOT
					type = airspace_convention
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_zeppelin_destination
		}
	}

	option = {	#A national tour
		name = curtiss.511.g
		default_option = yes
		curtiss_add_1_flight_route = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = curtiss_hindenburg_national_modifier
			days = 365
		}
	}

	option = {	#An international tour
		name = curtiss.511.h
		trigger = {
			any_country = {
				has_diplomatic_pact = {
					who = ROOT
					type = airspace_convention
				}
			}
		}
		curtiss_add_1_flight_route = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = curtiss_hindenburg_international_modifier
			days = 365
		}
		scope:curtiss_zeppelin_destination = {
			change_relations = {
				country = ROOT 
				value = 5
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					curtiss_has_helium = no
				}
				random_list = { #First voyage should be safer
					85 = {
						trigger_event = {
							id = curtiss.512
							days = 365
						}
					}
					15 = {
						trigger_event = {
							id = curtiss.513
							days = { 100 200 }
							popup = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					curtiss_has_helium = yes
				}
				random_list = {
					98 = {
						trigger_event = {
							id = curtiss.512
							days = 365
						}
					}
					2 = {
						trigger_event = {
							id = curtiss.513
							days = { 100 200 }
							popup = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Curtiss 514: Helium instead of Hydrogen

curtiss.514 = {
	type = country_event

	title = curtiss.514.t

	desc = curtiss.514.d

	flavor = curtiss.514.f
	
	duration = 2

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/curtiss_pictures/curtiss_zeppelin.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_zeppelin.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airship"

	trigger = {
		has_modifier = curtiss_hindenburg_build_modifier
		curtiss_has_helium = yes 
		NOT = {
			has_variable = curtiss_zeppelin_helium_var
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = curtiss_zeppelin_helium_var
	}

	option = {	#Perfect
		name = curtiss.514.g
		default_option = yes
	}
}

######ZEPPELIN EXPEDITION######

#Curtiss 520: Choose Zeppelin Expedition Leader

curtiss.520 = {
	type = country_event

    title = curtiss.520.t
    desc = curtiss.520.d
    flavor = curtiss.520.f

    event_image = {
		video = "gfx/event_pictures/unspecififc_airship.bk2"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_zeppelin.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airship"

    duration = 3

	immediate = {
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = curtiss_pilot
					has_trait = curtiss_pilot_ace
				}
				is_busy = no
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_expedition_leader_1
		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = curtiss_pilot
					has_trait = curtiss_pilot_ace
				}
				NOT = {
					this = scope:curtiss_expedition_leader_1
				}
				is_busy = no
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_expedition_leader_2
		}
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = curtiss_pilot
					has_trait = curtiss_pilot_ace
				}
				NOT = {
					this = scope:curtiss_expedition_leader_1
				}
				NOT = {
					this = scope:curtiss_expedition_leader_2
				}
				is_busy = no
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_expedition_leader_3
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = curtiss.520.g
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:curtiss_expedition_leader_1
		}
		scope:curtiss_expedition_leader_1 = {
			set_variable = curtiss_expedition_leader_var
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = curtiss.520.h
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:curtiss_expedition_leader_2
		}
		scope:curtiss_expedition_leader_2 = {
			set_variable = curtiss_expedition_leader_var
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = curtiss.520.i
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:curtiss_expedition_leader_3
		}
		scope:curtiss_expedition_leader_3 = {
			set_variable = curtiss_expedition_leader_var
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = yes
		}
	}

	after = {
		trigger_event = {
			id = curtiss.521
			days = { 3 7 }
		}
	}
}

#Curtiss 523: Expedition returns with success

curtiss.523 = {
	type = country_event

	title = curtiss.523.t

	desc = curtiss.523.d

	flavor = curtiss.523.f
	
	duration = 2

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/curtiss_pictures/curtiss_zeppelin_arctic.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_zeppelin.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airship"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		remove_modifier = curtiss_zeppelin_expedition_cost_modifier
		remove_modifier = curtiss_arctica_expedition_modifier
		curtiss_add_1_zeppelin_science = yes
	}

	option = {	#Welcome back
		name = curtiss.523.g
		default_option = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = curtiss_had_arctica_expedition_modifier
			years = 3
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:curtiss_zeppelin_science <= 1
				has_variable = curtiss_zeppelin_geography_var
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_zeppelin_geography_small_modifier
				years = 3
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:curtiss_zeppelin_science <= 1
				has_variable = curtiss_zeppelin_meteorology_var
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_zeppelin_meteorology_small_modifier
				years = 3
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:curtiss_zeppelin_science <= 1
				has_variable = curtiss_zeppelin_biology_var
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_zeppelin_biology_small_modifier
				years = 3
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:curtiss_zeppelin_science >= 2
				var:curtiss_zeppelin_science <= 4
				has_variable = curtiss_zeppelin_geography_var
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_zeppelin_geography_medium_modifier
				years = 3
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:curtiss_zeppelin_science >= 2
				var:curtiss_zeppelin_science <= 4
				has_variable = curtiss_zeppelin_meteorology_var
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_zeppelin_meteorology_medium_modifier
				years = 3
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:curtiss_zeppelin_science >= 2
				var:curtiss_zeppelin_science <= 4
				has_variable = curtiss_zeppelin_biology_var
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_zeppelin_biology_medium_modifier
				years = 3
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:curtiss_zeppelin_science >= 5
				has_variable = curtiss_zeppelin_geography_var
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_zeppelin_geography_large_modifier
				years = 3
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:curtiss_zeppelin_science >= 5
				has_variable = curtiss_zeppelin_meteorology_var
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_zeppelin_meteorology_large_modifier
				years = 3
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:curtiss_zeppelin_science >= 5
				has_variable = curtiss_zeppelin_biology_var
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = curtiss_zeppelin_biology_large_modifier
				years = 3
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		remove_variable = curtiss_zeppelin_geography_var
		remove_variable = curtiss_zeppelin_meteorology_var
		remove_variable = curtiss_zeppelin_biology_var
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = curtiss_expedition_leader_var
			}
			remove_variable = curtiss_expedition_leader_var
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = no 
		}
	}
}

#Curtiss 524: Expedition disaster

curtiss.524 = {
	type = country_event

	title = curtiss.524.t

	desc = curtiss.524.d

	flavor = curtiss.524.f
	
	duration = 2

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/curtiss_pictures/curtiss_zeppelin_arctic.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_zeppelin.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airship"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		remove_modifier = curtiss_zeppelin_expedition_cost_modifier
		remove_modifier = curtiss_arctica_expedition_modifier
	}

	option = {	#This is a tragedy
		name = curtiss.524.g
		add_modifier = {
			name = curtiss_had_arctica_expedition_modifier
			years = 3
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = curtiss_arctica_expedition_disaster_modifier
			years = 3
		}
		random_list = {
			75 = {
				trigger_event = {
					id = curtiss.525
					days = { 14 21 }
				}
			}
			25 = {
				trigger_event = {
					id = curtiss.526
					days = { 14 21 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#We need a rescue mission!
		name = curtiss.524.h
		default_option = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = curtiss_had_arctica_expedition_modifier
			years = 3
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = curtiss_arctica_expedition_disaster_modifier
			years = 3
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = curtiss_arctica_rescue_mission_modifier
			years = 3
		}
		add_treasury = -25000
		random_list = {
			35 = {
				trigger_event = {
					id = curtiss.525
					days = { 14 21 }
				}
			}
			65 = {
				trigger_event = {
					id = curtiss.526
					days = { 14 21 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		remove_variable = curtiss_zeppelin_geography_var
		remove_variable = curtiss_zeppelin_meteorology_var
		remove_variable = curtiss_zeppelin_biology_var
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = curtiss_expedition_leader_var
			}
			remove_variable = curtiss_expedition_leader_var
			set_character_busy_and_immortal = no 
		}
	}
}

			has_global_variable = curtiss_north_pole_passage
		}
		has_variable = curtiss_zeppelin_geography_var

	}

		}
	}

		curtiss_add_1_zeppelin_science = yes
		add_modifier = {
			name = curtiss_zeppelin_north_pole_modifier
		}
		scope:curtiss_expedition_leader = {
			add_trait = explorer
		}
	}
}

						limit = {
							scope:curtiss_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = curtiss_pilot_ace
							}
						}
					}
					add = -10
				}
				modifier = {

						limit = {

						}
					}
					add = -10
				}

			}
		}
	}

		name = curtiss.533.h

		curtiss_add_1_zeppelin_progress = yes
	}

	after = {
	}

	option = {	#Try to get us out of harm's way, whatever the cost!
		name = curtiss.535.h
		curtiss_add_1_zeppelin_danger = yes
		curtiss_sub_3_zeppelin_progress = yes
	}

	option = {	#$PILOT$ will save the day
		name = curtiss.535.i
		trigger = {
			scope:curtiss_expedition_leader = {
				has_trait = curtiss_pilot_ace
			}
		}
		default_option = yes
		curtiss_sub_1_zeppelin_progress = yes
	}
}

	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airship"

	}

	immediate = {
		curtiss_add_1_zeppelin_progress = yes
	}

	option = {	#A good place for a rest.
		name = curtiss.538.g
		default_option = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:curtiss_zeppelin_danger >= 1
			}
			curtiss_sub_1_zeppelin_danger = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:curtiss_zeppelin_danger = 0
			}
			curtiss_add_1_zeppelin_science = yes
		}
	}

	option = {	#We should establish a permanent research station.
		name = curtiss.538.h
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_modifier = curtiss_polar_station_modifier
			}
		}
		add_modifier = {
			name = curtiss_polar_station_modifier
		}
	}
}

######BALLOONEERING######

#Curtiss 600: Balloon flight from Vauxhall Gardens to Weilburg
curtiss.600 = {
	type = country_event

	title = curtiss.600.t

	desc = curtiss.600.d

	flavor = curtiss.600.f
	
	duration = 2

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/curtiss_pictures/curtiss_royal_vauxhall.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_ballooning.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airship"

	trigger = {
		exists = c:GBR
		c:GBR = root
		NOT = {
			has_global_variable = curtiss_royal_fauxhall_global_var
		}
		game_date > 1835.11.1
	}

	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = curtiss_royal_fauxhall_global_var

		set_variable = {
			name = new_balloon_time_var #for setting the record of the longest flight
			value = 18
		}
		curtiss_balloon_country_time_record_effect = yes
	}

	option = {	#Another record for Great Britain!
		name = curtiss.600.g
		default_option = yes

		big_curtiss_ballooning_research_effect = yes
	}
}

#Curtiss 601: Invention of the Rip Panel
curtiss.601 = {
	type = country_event

	title = curtiss.601.t

	desc = curtiss.601.d

	flavor = curtiss.601.f
	
	duration = 2

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/curtiss_pictures/curtiss_john_wise.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_ballooning.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airship"

	trigger = {
		exists = c:USA
		c:USA = root
		NOT = {
			has_global_variable = curtiss_rip_panel_invented_global_var
		}
		game_date > 1839.04.27
	}

	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = curtiss_rip_panel_invented_global_var

		create_character = {
			template = mr_usa_wise_john_character_template

			save_scope_as = curtiss_balloonist_scope
		}
	}

	option = {	#Great work! Hopefully we will hear of this guy again!
		name = curtiss.601.g
		default_option = yes

		big_curtiss_ballooning_research_effect = yes
	}

	option = {	#Actually, we need a new balloonist!
		name = curtiss.601.h

		custom_tooltip = {
			text = curtiss.601.h.tt
	
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = curtiss_balloonist_var
				}
				kill_balloonist_effect = yes
			}

			scope:curtiss_balloonist_scope = {
				set_variable = curtiss_john_wise_character_var
				set_variable = mr_is_balloonist_var
				place_character_in_void = 1200
				set_variable = {
					name = curtiss_balloonist_experience_var
					value = 150
				}
			}
				
			set_variable = {
				name = curtiss_balloonist_var
				value = scope:curtiss_balloonist_scope
			}
		
			set_variable = {
				name = curtiss_balloon_name_randomizer_var
				value = { 1 25 }
			}
		
			round_variable = {
				name = curtiss_balloon_name_randomizer_var
				nearest = 1
			}
		}

		big_curtiss_ballooning_research_effect = yes
	}
}

#Curtiss 603: Francisque Arban disappeared during a balloon flight over the Mediterranean Sea
curtiss.603 = {
	type = country_event

	title = curtiss.603.t

	desc = curtiss.603.d

	flavor = curtiss.603.f
	
	duration = 2

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/curtiss_pictures/curtiss_francisque_arban.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_ballooning.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airship"

	trigger = {
		exists = c:FRA
		c:FRA = root
		has_global_variable = curtiss_arban_alps_global_var
		NOT = {
			has_global_variable = curtiss_arban_mediterranean_lost_global_var
		}
		game_date > 1849.09.02
	}

	immediate = {
		set_global_variable = curtiss_arban_mediterranean_lost_global_var
	}

	option = {	#Horrible! Send out ships to search him!
		name = curtiss.603.g
		default_option = yes

		add_treasury = -20000

		add_modifier = {
			name = curtiss_arban_lost_modifier
			months = 24
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				3 = {
					trigger_event = {
						id = curtiss.604
						days = { 2 21 }
					}
					set_variable = curtiss_searching_arban_mediterranean
				}
				2 = {
					trigger_event = {
						id = curtiss.605
						years = 4
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#It was a risk he was willing to take...
		name = curtiss.603.h

		add_modifier = {
			name = curtiss_arban_lost_modifier
			months = 24
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				1 = {
					trigger_event = {
						id = curtiss.604
						days = { 2 21 }
					}
				}
				9 = {
					trigger_event = {
						id = curtiss.605
						years = 4
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Curtiss 605: Extra: Arban enslaved in Africa!
curtiss.605 = {
	type = country_event

	title = curtiss.605.t

	desc = curtiss.605.d

	flavor = curtiss.605.f
	
	duration = 2

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/curtiss_pictures/curtiss_arban_slave.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_ballooning.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airship"

	trigger = {
		any_country = {
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_law = law_type:law_debt_slavery
					has_law = law_type:law_slave_trade
					has_law = law_type:law_legacy_slavery
				}
				OR = {
					has_state_in_state_region = STATE_ALGIERS
					has_state_in_state_region = STATE_CONSTANTINE
					has_state_in_state_region = STATE_EAST_SAHARA
					has_state_in_state_region = STATE_FEZ
					has_state_in_state_region = STATE_INNER_MOROCCO
					has_state_in_state_region = STATE_LIBYA
					has_state_in_state_region = STATE_LIBYAN_DESERT
					has_state_in_state_region = STATE_MARRAKECH
					has_state_in_state_region = STATE_SAHARA
					has_state_in_state_region = STATE_ORAN
					has_state_in_state_region = STATE_TRIPOLI
					has_state_in_state_region = STATE_TUNISIA
					has_state_in_state_region = STATE_WEST_SAHARA
					has_state_in_state_region = STATE_AL_RIF
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
	}

	option = {	#We have to find Arban!
		name = curtiss.605.g
		default_option = yes

		add_modifier = {
			name = curtiss_searching_arban_modifier
			months = 12
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				3 = {
					trigger_event = {
						id = curtiss.606
						days = { 30 180 }
					}
				}
				2 = {
					trigger_event = {
						id = curtiss.608
						months = { 6 11 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Those are stories no one should believe.
		name = curtiss.605.h

		add_radicals = {
			value = 0.01
			strata = rich
		} 
	}
}

#Curtiss 606: Arban was enslaved in SCOPE
curtiss.606 = {
	type = country_event

	title = curtiss.606.t

	desc = curtiss.606.d

	flavor = curtiss.606.f
	
	duration = 2

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/curtiss_pictures/curtiss_arban_slave.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_ballooning.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airship"

	trigger = {
		any_country = {
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_law = law_type:law_debt_slavery
					has_law = law_type:law_slave_trade
					has_law = law_type:law_legacy_slavery
				}
				OR = {
					has_state_in_state_region = STATE_ALGIERS
					has_state_in_state_region = STATE_CONSTANTINE
					has_state_in_state_region = STATE_EAST_SAHARA
					has_state_in_state_region = STATE_FEZ
					has_state_in_state_region = STATE_INNER_MOROCCO
					has_state_in_state_region = STATE_LIBYA
					has_state_in_state_region = STATE_LIBYAN_DESERT
					has_state_in_state_region = STATE_MARRAKECH
					has_state_in_state_region = STATE_SAHARA
					has_state_in_state_region = STATE_ORAN
					has_state_in_state_region = STATE_TRIPOLI
					has_state_in_state_region = STATE_TUNISIA
					has_state_in_state_region = STATE_WEST_SAHARA
					has_state_in_state_region = STATE_AL_RIF
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					OR = {
						has_law = law_type:law_debt_slavery
						has_law = law_type:law_slave_trade
						has_law = law_type:law_legacy_slavery
					}
					OR = {
						has_state_in_state_region = STATE_ALGIERS
						has_state_in_state_region = STATE_CONSTANTINE
						has_state_in_state_region = STATE_EAST_SAHARA
						has_state_in_state_region = STATE_FEZ
						has_state_in_state_region = STATE_INNER_MOROCCO
						has_state_in_state_region = STATE_LIBYA
						has_state_in_state_region = STATE_LIBYAN_DESERT
						has_state_in_state_region = STATE_MARRAKECH
						has_state_in_state_region = STATE_SAHARA
						has_state_in_state_region = STATE_ORAN
						has_state_in_state_region = STATE_TRIPOLI
						has_state_in_state_region = STATE_TUNISIA
						has_state_in_state_region = STATE_WEST_SAHARA
						has_state_in_state_region = STATE_AL_RIF
					}
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_arban_slaver_scope
		}
	}

	option = {	#We will free him from his captors!
		name = curtiss.606.g
		default_option = yes

		scope:curtiss_arban_slaver_scope = {
			change_relations = {
				country = root
				value = -20
			}
		}

		set_variable = curtiss_force_freed_arban_var

		trigger_event = {
			id = curtiss.607
			days = 7
		}
	}

	option = {	#Let us just pay and get this over with...
		name = curtiss.606.h

		add_treasury = -50000
		
		add_radicals = {
			value = 0.02
			pop_type = academics
		}

		trigger_event = {
			id = curtiss.607
			days = 7
		}
	}
}

#Curtiss 614: Auguste Piccard considers moving to Brussels
curtiss.614 = {
	type = country_event

	title = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				NOT = {
					any_country = {
						country_is_in_europe = yes
						any_scope_building = {
							is_building_type = building_university
							level >= 20
						}
					}
				}
			}
			desc = curtiss.614.t_brussels
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				any_country = {
					country_is_in_europe = yes
					any_scope_building = {
						is_building_type = building_university
						level >= 20
					}
				}
			}
			desc = curtiss.614.t_capital
		}
	}

	desc = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				NOT = {
					any_country = {
						country_is_in_europe = yes
						any_scope_building = {
							is_building_type = building_university
							level >= 20
						}
					}
				}
			}
			desc = curtiss.614.d_brussels
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				any_country = {
					country_is_in_europe = yes
					any_scope_building = {
						is_building_type = building_university
						level >= 20
					}
				}
			}
			desc = curtiss.614.d_capital
		}
	}

	flavor = curtiss.614.f
	
	duration = 2

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/curtiss_pictures/curtiss_auguste_piccard.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_ballooning.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airship"

	trigger = {
		exists = c:SWI
		c:SWI = root
		NOT = {
			has_global_variable = curtiss_auguste_piccard_global_var
		}
		game_date = 1822.05.07
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_country = {
					country_is_in_europe = yes
					any_scope_building = {
						is_building_type = building_university
						level >= 20
					}
				}
			}
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					country_is_in_europe = yes
					any_scope_building = {
						is_building_type = building_university
						level >= 20
					}
				}
			}
			save_scope_as = curtiss_august_piccard_destination
		}
		else = {
			p:x018061 = {
				owner = {
					save_scope_as = curtiss_august_piccard_destination
				}
			}
		}

		set_global_variable = curtiss_auguste_piccard_global_var

		create_character = {
			template = mr_swi_piccard_auguste_character_template

			save_scope_as = curtiss_balloonist_scope
		}

		scope:curtiss_balloonist_scope = {
			set_variable = curtiss_auguste_piccard_character_var
			set_variable = mr_is_balloonist_var
			place_character_in_void = 1200
		}
	}

	option = {	#We can't lose Piccard offer to sponsor him!
		name = curtiss.614.g
		default_option = yes

		add_treasury = -100000

		custom_tooltip = {
			text = curtiss.614.g.tt
	
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = curtiss_balloonist_var
				}
				kill_balloonist_effect = yes
			}

			scope:curtiss_balloonist_scope = {
				set_variable = {
					name = curtiss_balloonist_experience_var
					value = 150
				}
			}
				
			set_variable = {
				name = curtiss_balloonist_var
				value = scope:curtiss_balloonist_scope
			}
		
			set_variable = {
				name = curtiss_balloon_name_randomizer_var
				value = { 1 25 }
			}
		
			round_variable = {
				name = curtiss_balloon_name_randomizer_var
				nearest = 1
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				trigger = {
					gold_reserves >= 200000
				}
				add = 100
			}	
		}
	}

	option = {	#We already have a great balloonist!
		name = curtiss.614.h
		default_option = yes

		scope:curtiss_august_piccard_destination = {
			trigger_event = curtiss.615
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 200
			modifier = {
				trigger = {
					gold_reserves >= 200000
				}
				add = -100
			}	
		}
	}
}

#Curtiss 615: Auguste Piccard moves to Capital / Brussels
curtiss.615 = {
	type = country_event

	title = curtiss.615.t
	desc = curtiss.615.d
	flavor = curtiss.615.f
	
	duration = 2

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:curtiss_balloonist_scope

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_ballooning.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	trigger = {
		#triggered by curtiss.614
	}

	immediate = {
	}

	option = {	#A balloonist of this renown should become our official Balloonist!
		name = curtiss.615.g
		default_option = yes

		custom_tooltip = {
			text = curtiss.615.g.tt
	
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = curtiss_balloonist_var
				}
				kill_balloonist_effect = yes
			}

			scope:curtiss_balloonist_scope = {
				set_variable = {
					name = curtiss_balloonist_experience_var
					value = 150
				}
			}
				
			set_variable = {
				name = curtiss_balloonist_var
				value = scope:curtiss_balloonist_scope
			}
		
			set_variable = {
				name = curtiss_balloon_name_randomizer_var
				value = { 1 25 }
			}
		
			round_variable = {
				name = curtiss_balloon_name_randomizer_var
				nearest = 1
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
	}

	option = {	#We wish him luck with his career!
		name = curtiss.615.h
		default_option = yes

		scope:curtiss_balloonist_scope = {
			free_character_from_void = no
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

#Curtiss 651: Ballooning in our country
curtiss.651 = {
	type = country_event

	title = curtiss.651.t

	desc = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = curtiss_balloonist_var
			}
			desc = curtiss.651.balloonist
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = curtiss_balloonist_var
				}
			}
			desc = curtiss.651.noballoonist
		}
	}

	flavor = curtiss.651.f
	
	duration = 2

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:curtiss_balloonist_scope

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_ballooning.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airship"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		var:curtiss_balloonist_var = {
			save_scope_as = curtiss_balloonist_scope
		}

		set_up_records_je_effect = yes

		balloonist_level_up_effect = yes
	}

	option = {	#Sponsor a balloonist!
		name = curtiss.651.g
		
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_variable = curtiss_balloonist_var
			}
		}

		trigger_event = {
			id = curtiss.650
			popup = yes
		}
	}

	option = {	#Stop sponsoring your balloonist
		name = curtiss.651.h
		
		trigger = {
			has_variable = curtiss_balloonist_var
		}

		kill_balloonist_effect = yes

		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = curtiss.651
				popup = yes
			}
		}

		custom_tooltip = curtiss.651.htt
	}

	option = {	#I don't want to hear about the flights of my balloonist anymore!
		name = curtiss.651.w

		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_variable = curtiss_no_balloonist_flight_events
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = curtiss.651
				popup = yes
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = curtiss.651.w.tt

		set_variable = curtiss_no_balloonist_flight_events
	}

	option = {	#Actually... Tell me about the flights of my balloonist again!
		name = curtiss.651.x

		trigger = {
			has_variable = curtiss_no_balloonist_flight_events
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = curtiss.651
				popup = yes
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = curtiss.651.x.tt

		remove_variable = curtiss_no_balloonist_flight_events
	}

	option = {	#If my balloonist dies just sponsor a new one without asking me.
		name = curtiss.651.y

		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_variable = curtiss_no_balloonist_death_events
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = curtiss.651
				popup = yes
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = curtiss.651.y.tt

		set_variable = curtiss_no_balloonist_death_events
	}

	option = {	#Tell me about the balloonist's deaths again and let me decide whether to sponsor a new one.
		name = curtiss.651.z

		trigger = {
			has_variable = curtiss_no_balloonist_death_events
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = curtiss.651
				popup = yes
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = curtiss.651.z.tt

		remove_variable = curtiss_no_balloonist_death_events
	}

	option = {	#Let me get back to my business!
		name = curtiss.651.l
		default_option = yes
	}
}

#Curtiss 652: Balloonist's first flight
curtiss.652 = {
	type = country_event

	title = curtiss.652.t

	desc = curtiss.652.d

	flavor = curtiss.652.f
	
	duration = 2

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:curtiss_balloonist_scope

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_ballooning.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/airship"

	trigger = {
		has_variable = curtiss_balloonist_var
		OR = {
			var:curtiss_balloon_altitude_record_var = 0
			var:curtiss_balloon_distance_record_var = 0
			var:curtiss_balloon_time_record_var = 0
		}
		NOT = { #only happens if player wants to see results.
			has_variable = curtiss_no_balloonist_flight_events
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		var:curtiss_balloonist_var = {
			save_scope_as = curtiss_balloonist_scope
		}

		curtiss_new_balloon_altitude_effect = yes
		curtiss_new_balloon_distance_effect = yes
		curtiss_new_balloon_time_effect = yes
	}

	option = {	#That's a good start!
		name = curtiss.652.g
		default_option = yes

		curtiss_balloon_country_altitude_experience_only_world_record_effect = yes
		curtiss_balloon_country_distance_record_experience_only_world_record_effect = yes
		curtiss_balloon_country_time_record_experience_only_world_record_effect = yes

		curtiss_ballooning_research_if_record_all_effect = yes

		balloonist_level_up_effect = yes
	}

	option = {	#I don't want to hear about the flights of my balloonist anymore!
		name = curtiss.651.w

		trigger = {
			is_player = yes
		}

		custom_tooltip = curtiss.651.w.tt

		set_variable = curtiss_no_balloonist_flight_events

		curtiss_balloon_country_altitude_experience_only_world_record_effect = yes
		curtiss_balloon_country_distance_record_experience_only_world_record_effect = yes
		curtiss_balloon_country_time_record_experience_only_world_record_effect = yes

		curtiss_ballooning_research_if_record_all_effect = yes

		balloonist_level_up_effect = yes

	}
}

#Curtiss 653: Balloonist tries to set new Altitude record
curtiss.653 = {
	type = country_event

	title = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				curtiss_altitude_record_country_broken_trigger = no
			}
			desc = curtiss.653.t1
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				curtiss_altitude_record_country_broken_trigger = yes
				curtiss_altitude_record_global_broken_trigger = no
			}
			desc = curtiss.653.t2
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				curtiss_altitude_record_global_broken_trigger = yes
			}
			desc = curtiss.653.t3
		}
	}

	desc = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				curtiss_altitude_record_country_broken_trigger = no
			}
			desc = curtiss.653.d1
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				curtiss_altitude_record_country_broken_trigger = yes
				curtiss_altitude_record_global_broken_trigger = no
			}
			desc = curtiss.653.d2
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				curtiss_altitude_record_global_broken_trigger = yes
			}
			desc = curtiss.653.d3
		}
	}

	flavor = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				curtiss_altitude_record_country_broken_trigger = no
			}
			desc = curtiss.653.f1
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				curtiss_altitude_record_country_broken_trigger = yes
				curtiss_altitude_record_global_broken_trigger = no
			}
			desc = curtiss.653.f2
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				curtiss_altitude_record_global_broken_trigger = yes
			}
			desc = curtiss.653.f3
		}
	}
	
	duration = 2

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:curtiss_balloonist_scope

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_ballooning.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	trigger = {
		#triggered by on_action in journal entry
		has_variable = curtiss_balloonist_var
		NOT = { #only happens if player wants to see results.
			has_variable = curtiss_no_balloonist_flight_events
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		curtiss_new_balloon_altitude_effect = yes

		var:curtiss_balloonist_var = {
			save_scope_as = curtiss_balloonist_scope
		}
	}

	option = {	#Good luck for next time!
		name = curtiss.653.g
		default_option = yes

		trigger = {
			curtiss_altitude_record_country_broken_trigger = no
		}

		small_curtiss_ballooning_research_effect = yes
		curtiss_balloon_country_altitude_record_effect = yes

		balloonist_level_up_effect = yes
	}

	option = {	#I don't want to hear about the flights of my balloonist anymore!
		name = curtiss.651.w

		trigger = {
			is_player = yes
			curtiss_altitude_record_country_broken_trigger = no
		}

		custom_tooltip = curtiss.651.w.tt

		set_variable = curtiss_no_balloonist_flight_events

		small_curtiss_ballooning_research_effect = yes
		curtiss_balloon_country_altitude_record_effect = yes

		balloonist_level_up_effect = yes
	}

	option = {	#Good job!
		name = curtiss.653.h

		trigger = {
			curtiss_altitude_record_country_broken_trigger = yes
			curtiss_altitude_record_global_broken_trigger = no
		}

		medium_curtiss_ballooning_research_effect = yes
		curtiss_balloon_country_altitude_record_effect = yes

		balloonist_level_up_effect = yes
	}

	option = {	#I don't want to hear about the flights of my balloonist anymore!
		name = curtiss.651.w

		trigger = {
			is_player = yes
			curtiss_altitude_record_country_broken_trigger = yes
			curtiss_altitude_record_global_broken_trigger = no
		}

		custom_tooltip = curtiss.651.w.tt

		set_variable = curtiss_no_balloonist_flight_events

		medium_curtiss_ballooning_research_effect = yes
		curtiss_balloon_country_altitude_record_effect = yes

		balloonist_level_up_effect = yes
	}

	option = {	#Wonderful! Congratulations!
		name = curtiss.653.i

		trigger = {
			curtiss_altitude_record_global_broken_trigger = yes
		}

		big_curtiss_ballooning_research_effect = yes
		curtiss_balloon_country_altitude_record_effect = yes

		balloonist_level_up_effect = yes
	}

	option = {	#I don't want to hear about the flights of my balloonist anymore!
		name = curtiss.651.w

		trigger = {
			is_player = yes
			curtiss_altitude_record_global_broken_trigger = yes
		}

		custom_tooltip = curtiss.651.w.tt

		set_variable = curtiss_no_balloonist_flight_events

		big_curtiss_ballooning_research_effect = yes
		curtiss_balloon_country_altitude_record_effect = yes

		balloonist_level_up_effect = yes
	}
}

#Curtiss 654: Balloonist tries to set new Distance record
curtiss.654 = {
	type = country_event

	title = curtiss.654.t

	desc = curtiss.654.d

	flavor = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				curtiss_distance_record_country_broken_trigger = no
				curtiss_time_record_country_broken_trigger = no
			}
			desc = curtiss.654.f1
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				curtiss_distance_record_global_broken_trigger = no
				curtiss_time_record_global_broken_trigger = no
				OR = {
					curtiss_distance_record_country_broken_trigger = yes
					curtiss_time_record_country_broken_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			desc = curtiss.654.f2
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					curtiss_distance_record_global_broken_trigger = yes
					curtiss_time_record_global_broken_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			desc = curtiss.654.f3
		}
	}
	
	duration = 2

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:curtiss_balloonist_scope

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_ballooning.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	trigger = {
		#triggered by on_action in journal entry
		has_variable = curtiss_balloonist_var
		NOT = { #only happens if player wants to see results.
			has_variable = curtiss_no_balloonist_flight_events
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		curtiss_new_balloon_distance_effect = yes
		curtiss_new_balloon_time_effect = yes

		var:curtiss_balloonist_var = {
			save_scope_as = curtiss_balloonist_scope
		}
	}

	option = {	#Good luck next time!
		name = curtiss.654.g
		default_option = yes

		trigger = {
			curtiss_distance_record_country_broken_trigger = no
			curtiss_time_record_country_broken_trigger = no
		}

		small_curtiss_ballooning_research_effect = yes
		curtiss_balloon_country_distance_record_effect = yes
		curtiss_balloon_country_time_record_effect = yes
		balloonist_level_up_effect = yes
	}

	option = {	#I don't want to hear about the flights of my balloonist anymore!
		name = curtiss.651.w

		trigger = {
			is_player = yes
			curtiss_distance_record_country_broken_trigger = no
			curtiss_time_record_country_broken_trigger = no
		}

		custom_tooltip = curtiss.651.w.tt

		set_variable = curtiss_no_balloonist_flight_events

		small_curtiss_ballooning_research_effect = yes
		curtiss_balloon_country_distance_record_effect = yes
		curtiss_balloon_country_time_record_effect = yes

		balloonist_level_up_effect = yes
	}

	option = {	#Good job!
		name = curtiss.654.h

		trigger = {
			curtiss_distance_record_global_broken_trigger = no
			curtiss_time_record_global_broken_trigger = no
			OR = {
				curtiss_distance_record_country_broken_trigger = yes
				curtiss_time_record_country_broken_trigger = yes
			}
		}

		medium_curtiss_ballooning_research_effect = yes
		curtiss_balloon_country_distance_record_effect = yes
		curtiss_balloon_country_time_record_effect = yes

		balloonist_level_up_effect = yes
	}

	option = {	#I don't want to hear about the flights of my balloonist anymore!
		name = curtiss.651.w

		trigger = {
			is_player = yes
			curtiss_distance_record_global_broken_trigger = no
			curtiss_time_record_global_broken_trigger = no
			OR = {
				curtiss_distance_record_country_broken_trigger = yes
				curtiss_time_record_country_broken_trigger = yes
			}
		}

		custom_tooltip = curtiss.651.w.tt

		set_variable = curtiss_no_balloonist_flight_events

		medium_curtiss_ballooning_research_effect = yes
		curtiss_balloon_country_distance_record_effect = yes
		curtiss_balloon_country_time_record_effect = yes

		balloonist_level_up_effect = yes
	}

	option = {	#Wonderful! Congratulations!
		name = curtiss.654.i

		trigger = {
			OR = {
				curtiss_distance_record_global_broken_trigger = yes
				curtiss_time_record_global_broken_trigger = yes
			}
		}

		big_curtiss_ballooning_research_effect = yes
		curtiss_balloon_country_distance_record_effect = yes
		curtiss_balloon_country_time_record_effect = yes

		balloonist_level_up_effect = yes
	}

	option = {	#I don't want to hear about the flights of my balloonist anymore!
		name = curtiss.651.w

		trigger = {
			is_player = yes
			OR = {
				curtiss_distance_record_global_broken_trigger = yes
				curtiss_time_record_global_broken_trigger = yes
			}
		}

		custom_tooltip = curtiss.651.w.tt

		set_variable = curtiss_no_balloonist_flight_events

		big_curtiss_ballooning_research_effect = yes
		curtiss_balloon_country_distance_record_effect = yes
		curtiss_balloon_country_time_record_effect = yes

		balloonist_level_up_effect = yes
	}
}

#Curtiss 656: Balloonist is afraid of heights and gives up ballooning
curtiss.656 = {
	type = country_event

	title = curtiss.656.t

	desc = curtiss.656.d

	flavor = curtiss.656.f
	
	duration = 1

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:curtiss_balloonist_scope

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_ballooning.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/destruction"

	trigger = {
		has_variable = curtiss_balloonist_var
	}

	immediate = {
		var:curtiss_balloonist_var = {
			save_scope_as = curtiss_balloonist_scope
		}
	}

	option = {	#How unfortunate...
		name = curtiss.656.g
		default_option = yes

		kill_balloonist_effect = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}

	option = {	#Argh! Is there another balloonist we could sponsor?
		name = curtiss.656.h

		kill_balloonist_effect = yes

		create_balloonist_effect = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

#Curtiss 657: Balloonist's first flight (hidden)
curtiss.657 = {
	type = country_event
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		has_variable = curtiss_balloonist_var
		OR = {
			var:curtiss_balloon_altitude_record_var = 0
			var:curtiss_balloon_distance_record_var = 0
			var:curtiss_balloon_time_record_var = 0
		}
		has_variable = curtiss_no_balloonist_flight_events
	}

	immediate = {
		curtiss_new_balloon_altitude_effect = yes
		curtiss_new_balloon_distance_effect = yes
		curtiss_new_balloon_time_effect = yes

		curtiss_balloon_country_altitude_experience_only_world_record_effect = yes
		curtiss_balloon_country_distance_record_experience_only_world_record_effect = yes
		curtiss_balloon_country_time_record_experience_only_world_record_effect = yes

		curtiss_ballooning_research_if_record_all_effect = yes

		balloonist_level_up_effect = yes
	}
}

#Curtiss 658: Balloonist tries to set new Altitude record (hidden)
curtiss.658 = {
	type = country_event
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		#triggered by on_action in journal entry
		has_variable = curtiss_balloonist_var
		has_variable = curtiss_no_balloonist_flight_events #only happens if player does not want to see events
	}

	immediate = {
		curtiss_new_balloon_altitude_effect = yes

		if = {
			limit = {
				curtiss_altitude_record_global_broken_trigger = yes
			}
			big_curtiss_ballooning_research_effect = yes
			curtiss_balloon_country_altitude_record_effect = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				curtiss_altitude_record_country_broken_trigger = yes
				curtiss_altitude_record_global_broken_trigger = no
			}

			medium_curtiss_ballooning_research_effect = yes
			curtiss_balloon_country_altitude_record_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			small_curtiss_ballooning_research_effect = yes
			curtiss_balloon_country_altitude_record_effect = yes
		}

		balloonist_level_up_effect = yes
	}
}

#Curtiss 659: Balloonist tries to set new Distance record (hidden)
curtiss.659 = {
	type = country_event
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		#triggered by on_action in journal entry
		has_variable = curtiss_balloonist_var
		has_variable = curtiss_no_balloonist_flight_events #only happens if player does not want to see events
	}

	immediate = {
		curtiss_new_balloon_distance_effect = yes
		curtiss_new_balloon_time_effect = yes

		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					curtiss_distance_record_global_broken_trigger = yes
					curtiss_time_record_global_broken_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			big_curtiss_ballooning_research_effect = yes
			curtiss_balloon_country_distance_record_effect = yes
			curtiss_balloon_country_time_record_effect = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				curtiss_distance_record_global_broken_trigger = no
				curtiss_time_record_global_broken_trigger = no
				OR = {
					curtiss_distance_record_country_broken_trigger = yes
					curtiss_time_record_country_broken_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			medium_curtiss_ballooning_research_effect = yes
			curtiss_balloon_country_distance_record_effect = yes
			curtiss_balloon_country_time_record_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			small_curtiss_ballooning_research_effect = yes
			curtiss_balloon_country_distance_record_effect = yes
			curtiss_balloon_country_time_record_effect = yes
		}

		balloonist_level_up_effect = yes
	}
}

#Curtiss 670: Balloonist died in accident
curtiss.670 = {
	type = country_event

	title = curtiss.670.t

	desc = curtiss.670.d

	flavor = curtiss.670.f
	
	duration = 1

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:curtiss_balloonist_scope

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_ballooning.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/destruction"

	trigger = { #triggered by journal entry
		has_variable = curtiss_balloonist_var
		NOT = { #prevents event from firing when player doesn't want to see it
			has_variable = curtiss_no_balloonist_death_events
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			var:curtiss_balloonist_var ?= {
				has_trait = curtiss_balloonist_experienced
			}
			factor = 0.85
		}
		modifier = {
			var:curtiss_balloonist_var ?= {
				has_trait = curtiss_balloonist_famous
			}
			factor = 0.75
		}
		modifier = {
			var:curtiss_balloonist_var ?= {
				has_trait = meticulous
			}
			factor = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {
			var:curtiss_balloonist_var ?= {
				has_trait = innovative
			}
			factor = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {
			var:curtiss_balloonist_var ?= {
				has_trait = opium_addiction
			}
			factor = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			var:curtiss_balloonist_var ?= {
				has_trait = alcoholic
			}
			factor = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			var:curtiss_balloonist_var ?= {
				has_trait = cocaine_addiction
			}
			factor = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			var:curtiss_balloonist_var ?= {
				has_trait = senile
			}
			factor = 4
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		var:curtiss_balloonist_var = {
			save_scope_as = curtiss_balloonist_scope
		}
	}

	option = {	#How horrible!
		name = curtiss.670.g
		default_option = yes

		kill_balloonist_effect = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}

	option = {	#Terrible! Is there another balloonist we could sponsor?
		name = curtiss.670.h

		kill_balloonist_effect = yes

		create_balloonist_effect = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

#Curtiss 671: Experienced Balloonist
curtiss.671 = {
	type = country_event

	title = curtiss.671.t

	desc = curtiss.671.d

	flavor = curtiss.671.f
	
	duration = 1

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:curtiss_balloonist_scope

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_ballooning.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/destruction"

	trigger = {
		has_variable = curtiss_balloonist_var
		has_variable = curtiss_no_balloonist_death_events
		var:curtiss_balloonist_var = {
			var:curtiss_balloonist_experience_var >= 100
			NOR = {
				has_trait = curtiss_balloonist_experienced
				has_trait = curtiss_balloonist_famous
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		var:curtiss_balloonist_var = {
			save_scope_as = curtiss_balloonist_scope
		}
	}

	option = {	#Good to hear
		name = curtiss.671.g
		default_option = yes

		var:curtiss_balloonist_var = {
			remove_trait = curtiss_balloonist
			add_trait = curtiss_balloonist_experienced
		}
	}
}

#Curtiss 672: Famous Balloonist
curtiss.672 = {
	type = country_event

	title = curtiss.672.t

	desc = curtiss.672.d

	flavor = curtiss.672.f
	
	duration = 1

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:curtiss_balloonist_scope

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_ballooning.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/destruction"

	trigger = {
		has_variable = curtiss_balloonist_var
		has_variable = curtiss_no_balloonist_death_events
		var:curtiss_balloonist_var = {
			var:curtiss_balloonist_experience_var >= 300
			NOT = {
				has_trait = curtiss_balloonist_famous
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		var:curtiss_balloonist_var = {
			save_scope_as = curtiss_balloonist_scope
		}
	}

	option = {	#Wonderful
		name = curtiss.672.g
		default_option = yes

		var:curtiss_balloonist_var = {
			remove_trait = curtiss_balloonist
			remove_trait = curtiss_balloonist_experienced
			add_trait = curtiss_balloonist_famous
		}
	}
}

#Curtiss 673: Balloonist killed by comet
curtiss.673 = {
	type = country_event

	title = curtiss.673.t

	desc = curtiss.673.d

	flavor = curtiss.673.f
	
	duration = 1

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/destruction"

	trigger = { #triggered by journal entry
		has_variable = curtiss_balloonist_var
		NOT = { #prevents event from firing when player doesn't want to see it
			has_variable = curtiss_no_balloonist_death_events
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 0.1
	}

	immediate = {
		var:curtiss_balloonist_var = {
			save_scope_as = curtiss_balloonist_scope
		}
	}

	option = {	#If he only had comet sense!
		name = curtiss.673.g
		default_option = yes

		kill_balloonist_effect = yes

		verrier_add_x_astronomical_objects_effect = {
			AMOUNT = 5
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}

	option = {	#Oh Comet, devil's kith and kin... Is there another balloonist we could sponsor?
		name = curtiss.673.h

		kill_balloonist_effect = yes

		create_balloonist_effect = yes

		verrier_add_x_astronomical_objects_effect = {
			AMOUNT = 5
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

curtiss.674 = {

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/destruction"

	trigger = { #triggered by journal entry
		has_variable = curtiss_balloonist_var
		NOT = { #prevents event from firing when player doesn't want to see it
			has_variable = curtiss_no_balloonist_death_events
		}
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 0.1
	}

		var:curtiss_balloonist_var = {
			save_scope_as = curtiss_balloonist_scope
		}
	}

	option = {	#How horrible!
		name = curtiss.674.g
		default_option = yes

		kill_balloonist_effect = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}

	option = {	#Terrible! Is there another balloonist we could sponsor?

		create_balloonist_effect = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

#Curtiss 675: Balloonist died in accident (hidden)
curtiss.675 = {
	type = country_event
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		has_variable = curtiss_balloonist_var
		has_variable = curtiss_no_balloonist_death_events
	}

	weight_multiplier = {
		base = 1
		modifier = {
			var:curtiss_balloonist_var ?= {
				has_trait = curtiss_balloonist_experienced
			}
			factor = 0.85
		}
		modifier = {
			var:curtiss_balloonist_var ?= {
				has_trait = curtiss_balloonist_famous
			}
			factor = 0.75
		}
		modifier = {
			var:curtiss_balloonist_var ?= {
				has_trait = meticulous
			}
			factor = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {
			var:curtiss_balloonist_var ?= {
				has_trait = innovative
			}
			factor = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {
			var:curtiss_balloonist_var ?= {
				has_trait = opium_addiction
			}
			factor = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			var:curtiss_balloonist_var ?= {
				has_trait = alcoholic
			}
			factor = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			var:curtiss_balloonist_var ?= {
				has_trait = cocaine_addiction
			}
			factor = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			var:curtiss_balloonist_var ?= {
				has_trait = senile
			}
			factor = 4
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		kill_balloonist_effect = yes

		create_balloonist_effect = yes
	}
}

#Curtiss 676: Our Balloonist died
curtiss.676 = {
	type = country_event

	title = curtiss.676.t

	desc = curtiss.676.d

#	flavor = curtiss.676.f
	
	duration = 3

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/academics_pictures/academics_academic_funeral.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_ballooning.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	trigger = {
		#Triggered by on_action in the journal
		NOT = { #prevents event from firing when player doesn't want to see it
			has_variable = curtiss_no_balloonist_death_events
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		remove_variable = curtiss_balloonist_var
	}

	option = {	#How horrible!
		name = curtiss.674.g
		default_option = yes

		kill_balloonist_effect = yes

		custom_tooltip = academics.11_tt

		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}

	option = {	#Terrible! Is there another balloonist we could sponsor?
		name = curtiss.674.h

		kill_balloonist_effect = yes

		create_balloonist_effect = yes

		custom_tooltip = academics.11_tt

		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}
